(Nanjing) Chiang Kai-shek ordered all localities to confiscate the assets of drug offenders and use them all as local opium suppression funds. (16th, Special Dispatch)

Jiangsu Provincial Women's Association Requests Ban on Women's Photo Advertisements

(Nanjing) According to a report by the Jiangsu Provincial Women's Association to the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Industry, commercial and industrial firms are using women's photos in their advertisements, which not only intentionally insults women but also features bizarre shapes and ugly poses, greatly impacting public morals. They request an order to prohibit this and to classify and ban it. The two ministries are currently in consultation. (16th, Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Requests Correction of False Pretenses of Banning Smoking

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan, based on a report from the Ministry of Finance, requested that the provincial governments be instructed, and also sent a letter to the Central Party Headquarters requesting that the provincial party departments be informed and instructed to order their subordinates to immediately correct any groups that use the name of the New Life Movement to prohibit people from selling or smoking cigarettes, in order to maintain national taxes and stabilize commerce. In addition to sending a letter to the secretary of the Central Executive Committee to forward it to the provincial party departments for investigation and action, it was also issued to all subordinates for unified compliance. (16th, Special Dispatch)

Judicial Yuan Explains Doubts Regarding the Petition Law

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan recently explained doubts regarding the Petition Law as follows: (1) Retired civil servants, regarding the amount and method of pension payments, are established according to the Civil Servant Pension Regulations for the special status of civil servants, and are actually public law rights. Therefore, after their request is rejected by the original office, regardless of whether they have suffered losses, they may not file a petition in accordance with Article 1 of the Petition Law. (2) When the government office accepting the petition believes that the petition is without reason, its decision should use the words "reject" or "repel." Although this is not explicitly stipulated in the Petition Law, in order to unify legal terminology, the word "reject" should be used in accordance with Article 8 of the same law. (16th, Central News Agency telegram)

Repairing the Tomb of Emperor Jing of Tang in Pucheng

(Xi'an) The Xi'an Office of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee has decided to repair the Tomb of Emperor Jing of Tang in Pucheng, because Emperor Xianzong of Tang was a wise ruler who restored the Tang Dynasty. (15th, Central News Agency telegram)

Jinpu Railway Improves Car Service

(Beiping) The Jinpu Improvement Committee has decided to implement the division of the entire railway's car and police services into six sections on July 1st to facilitate execution. (16th, Special Dispatch)

Disaster Situation Investigation in Zunhua Completed

(Beiping) The Hebei Civil Affairs Department has decided to allocate 2,000 yuan for disaster relief in Zunhua. The disaster situation in the county has already been investigated and clarified. A total of 41 villages have been affected, with over 500 households and 1,500 disaster victims. 600 houses were burned down, and over 50 people died. (16th, Special Dispatch)

(Chongqing) Pan Wenhua, following Chiang Kai-shek's instruction that military officers should not concurrently hold civilian posts, has resigned from the position of Mayor of Chongqing. Current Commentary

Economic Self-Reliance

— Duan

If China does not seek self-sufficiency, it will be impossible to ensure China's survival. However, while self-sufficiency is what our hearts desire, it is as difficult as ascending to heaven. This is not just because a planned economy is not easily realized at once. Even if it is realized, will those with hawkish eyes allow China to proceed leisurely without hindering or sabotaging it? Those who discuss economics, for the sake of developing the country's agriculture, industry, and commerce, do not just advocate increasing production to be self-sufficient but also to supply others, and to slightly reduce the outflow of foreign goods. They also advocate raising tariffs to protect the people and thus protect the country, and to temporarily resist the raging tide that has already collapsed. These theories have a deep and long history in economics, but under China's current circumstances, what is the actual situation? One cannot but give considerable thought to this. Taking the current situation as an example, in terms of agriculture, ten yuan per dan of silkworm cocoons, regardless of the cost of mulberry leaves, those raising silkworms calculate their income, which is probably even less than a Shanghai maid's monthly wage. Soybean and wheat harvests have been abundant and poor, but the selling price is difficult to exchange for three dou of rice per dan. Looking back at the soybeans transported from Dalian, they are still depreciating and encroaching on the market. Rice and wheat from across the ocean are still coming in continuously. Agricultural products, regardless of whether the harvest is abundant or poor, are all worthless, while nearly 70% of the daily necessities of farmers are foreign goods. How can the countryside not go bankrupt, and how can the cities not collapse? In terms of industry, to say something heartbreaking, almost everything seen in the market is a processed product made from foreign goods, or a product of foreign-owned factories within our country. Since tariffs were raised, many goods are imported from foreign countries as materials and assembled locally. Those who are unaware think that these so-called "Made in Shanghai" products must be domestic goods, but how can they know that they are foreign goods disguised to deceive people? As for heavy industry, it is even less to be discussed. If there is any, it is either jointly operated with foreigners or solely operated by foreigners. Light industry is occasionally started, but it is often subjected to foreign exclusion. Very few can stand on their own. Looking to the future, I want to seek self-sufficiency, but people do not allow me to be self-sufficient. What can I do?

As for tariff protection, it is effective in all countries, but in our country, tax evasion and smuggling are often heard of, and even armed transport disregards public opinion. Under this kind of situation, it is even more difficult to find an effective solution. Our products still have various domestic taxes. Now, they are in the same market as goods that are imported by evading taxes. Their failure can be expected. However, we should not allow people to invade our markets and control our profit sources because of the overwhelming difficulties, and not know how to seek survival. Calamities often build a nation. This is precisely the best time to test whether our nation can overcome this difficult situation.

Recently, the British government has dispatched Mr. Ross as the economic advisor to the British Ambassador to China to investigate, in order to revive our country's economy, especially focusing on monetary issues. France has also dispatched Mr. Renault-Xi, an expert on international monetary issues, to come to China together. According to a Reuter's dispatch from London on the 11th, when representatives from various countries studied China's monetary issues, they will maintain the silver standard used domestically, but negotiate a new method for foreign use. Generally, each country is based on its own technical standpoint. That is, Britain advocates that China's foreign currency should be linked to the pound, France advocates that it should be linked to gold, and the United States will require it to be linked to the dollar. What they say is difficult to believe before the various countries have expressed their opinions. However, since each has its own opinions, and there are conflicting interests, it is feared that it will be difficult to obtain good results. Moreover, there are still other obstacles. In short, when foreigners plan for China, they are planning for themselves, which is the norm of human nature. For example, Britain has huge railway claims in China, and China is also its major customer in Manchester. It cannot ignore the risk of its interests being damaged. However, we must always seek our own survival and not be dependent on others and be dominated by others. For example, the currency system has no reason to remain unchanged for a long time, but its change should always be based on our own standpoint, seeking less harm and more benefit, and lasting and feasible. If it is a temporary measure, regardless of the harm later, thinking that it is needed today and using it, and abandoning it tomorrow when it is not needed, I am afraid that it will not be so easy. Even if it is possible, the chaos and damage suffered by the general public would be unbearable. If it is like this, then why not declare to people that they should abandon their silver purchase policy? We know that it is ineffective, but it will not cause malpractices.

I believe that in this dangerous situation, to seek survival in the slightest chance, we can only do our best and plan for the overall situation. As for the differences in academic propositions, there seems to be no need to haggle over them. The ancients finished their discussions and the troops had already crossed the river. This can be a lesson for us. For example, the Shanghai financial incident was not without shocking waves and extreme danger. However, as a result of the joint efforts of all parties, it turned from danger to safety. Today, the financial organization has undergone many changes. If the effectiveness of the collection, concentration, and unification can be used well and gradually developed, how can we know that this panic will not turn into a better new situation?

In short, the key to improving China's economy lies in self-reliance. Others can plan for me, but I can only carefully choose among them. I can never accept it as a whole. However, how can we achieve self-reliance? This is what I hope that scholars and experts will exhaust their wisdom to study.

China at a Critical Juncture of Survival, National Unity is the First Priority, Sir Frederick Whyte Publishes an Article

(London) The Observer today published an article by Sir Frederick Whyte, former political advisor to the Chinese government, stating that China is currently in a critical period of survival, independently supporting the precarious situation. Forty years ago, the five major powers were jealous of each other and did not want any one country to excessively expand its power, so China was able to escape being divided. However, today, only one country is rampant in the Far East. China can only rely on its own passive resistance and national unity. Far-sighted Chinese should be aware of this difficult period and resolve to reorganize their internal affairs, cultivate and strengthen their national strength, and seek revival. (15th, Reuters telegram)

Moscow Newspaper Discusses the International Situation

(Moscow) An editorial in the Moscow Daily stated, "Since the end of the Great War and the establishment of the League of Nations, the world has never had such a wide range of choices between various methods of international relations, in policies leading to war and policies preserving peace. Collective security guarantees and joint action by the powers against aggressor nations are the fundamental ideas of the League of Nations. This has been clearly stated in Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the League of Nations Covenant.

However, facts have proven that the realization of this principle has repeatedly encountered serious difficulties. Therefore, the theory and implementation of the League of Nations must be limited, and the collective security guarantee realized through local conventions has become a continuation of the League of Nations' ideas. This limitation of ideas has been explained by life itself.

Indeed, countries that clearly understand the limitations of the path to peace will not abandon their aggression plans. When this guiding limitation begins to be realized, or when that guiding accelerates its aggression preparations, these countries will also begin to withdraw from the League of Nations. Their withdrawal from the League of Nations actually contains the meaning of attempting to destroy the collective security guarantee system.

Hitler's theory of localizing war is only a declaration to disperse world thought, and has the same meaning as admitting that aggression is not a crime. At this time, the whole world can see where Hitler's theory will lead.

China is the first victim of these League of Nations opponents and believers in the idea of localizing war. Japan, because it is considered innocent, can continue to invade China again and again, seeking to complete its ambition to destroy China's independence.

We are now seeing an ugly phenomenon: although the powers have also witnessed the path to peace and their own interests being repeatedly attacked, they have failed to achieve anything because they cannot unite and there is no agreement on how to deal with these events.

Hitler's idea of localizing war has long been adopted by Japan. Germany is still advocating it, but this is only because Germany of the National Socialist Party has not yet completed its military expansion and therefore feels that its strength is insufficient, so it can only temporarily not implement it.

"If European countries do not unite in time to prevent it, there will be such a day. If the only purpose of the Czech Foreign Minister's visit is to provide new proof of this truth, then its purpose has been achieved. We firmly believe that Pi's visit will be praised throughout Europe, except by those countries that believe in the localization of the German-Japanese war." (16th, TASS telegram)

Japanese Covet Philippine Island Chromium Ore

Manila News The general manager of the Palaras Mining Company and the Benguet Mining Company, which owns large amounts of "Ming" ore production, Mr. Housseman, recently told people that Japanese residing in the Philippines have used various friendly coercive means to try to obtain all of the Philippine Islands' potential chromium production, because chromium is a military material, and the Philippine Islands are one of the most important chromium producing areas. (World News Agency)

Oriental Clipper Arrives at Midway Island from Pearl Harbor

The Pan American Airlines flying boat Clipper, which recently flew 2,400 miles from San Francisco to Honolulu in seventeen hours and fifty-eight minutes, arrived at Midway Island at 1:40 AM this morning (Greenwich Mean Time). The island is the second of five aviation stations under construction in the Pacific for regular commercial aviation between the United States and China. This flight tested Clipper's power to navigate in unstable weather. (16th, Reuters telegram)

Japanese Minister of the Army Returns to Country Talks About Japanese-Russian Conflict Crisis Not Gone Admits Northeast Volunteer Army Forces Strong Not Easy to Eliminate Advocates Large-Scale Immigration to Manchuria Military Expenditure Cannot be Reduced

(Shimonoseki) Minister of the Army Hayashi, along with aides such as Nagata and Yokomizo, arrived here at 7:30 PM on the 15th, and boarded a special express train at 8:30 PM to head east. He is scheduled to arrive in Tokyo at 3:25 PM on the 16th. According to his remarks in Shimonoseki:

The Kwantung Army, with the Commander of the South as the center, is far from home. Without any complete equipment and without being comforted, its officers and soldiers are in a difficult situation, but they do not show any dissatisfaction and are able to serve with all their strength, which is really admirable. Although the major motive for war between the Soviet Union and "Manchukuo" has not yet been discovered, it is easy to create a motive for conflict, which is extremely important to pay attention to. Regarding maintaining治安, the Japanese and Manchurian armies should make every effort to plan it. It seems difficult to eliminate "bandits" in the short term. There are still many undeveloped places in Manchuria, so development is necessary for both Japan's population problem and the industrial development of "Manchukuo." Therefore, large-scale immigration must be carried out based on the national policy. The abolition of extraterritoriality is now in preparation, and the decision has been made to start with the abolition of taxation rights. The general method will be implemented by the end of "Kangde" Year Four. (16th, Japanese United News Agency telegram)

Vice Minister Miyahara Hashimoto greeted the Minister of the Army at Shizuoka Station at 0:37 PM on the 16th. On the train, he reported to the Minister of the Army all the circumstances during his trip to Manchuria, especially the attitude taken by the Army Central Department on the North China issue, the decisions of the Cabinet Deliberation Council, and other details. He also held important consultations regarding the Army Ministry's policy towards the Second Cabinet Deliberation Council on the 17th, and the North China issue, the Chahar issue, etc. (16th, Japanese Telegraph News)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota originally hoped to visit Manchuria for inspection, and because Counselor Tani and Minister of the Army Hayashi and others frequently persuaded the Foreign Minister to go to Manchuria, he has decided to go to Manchuria for inspection. Moreover, because there are many urgent issues such as the abolition of extraterritoriality and the establishment of additional consulates, and the disarmament preparatory negotiations will be held this autumn, the Foreign Minister's visit to Manchuria will be around August or September. At that time, Ambassador to the UK Matsudaira and Ambassador to Germany Mushakoji will also return to the country, or they will visit Manchuria together with the ambassadors. (16th, Electric Communications telegram)

Under the Iron Heel of the Japanese, Andong People Cannot Make a Living, 500,000 People Have Difficulty Maintaining Life, Suicides and Crimes are Endless

A Hua Lian News Agency dispatch from Andong reports that the Dongbian Road area, centered on Andong, has been suffering for years, and the people are in dire straits. In areas such as Hama Tang, Wulonggu, Stone City, Ji'an, Linjiang, Changbai, Sandaolangtou, Hunshuipao, Dadonggou, Dagushan, and Zhuanghe, there are currently 540,000 poor people on the verge of starvation. Because they cannot make a living, 5,000 people have moved to other places, 145 people have committed crimes due to poverty, and the most tragic thing is that recently there have been 55 suicide victims. 280 people sold all their forest properties to maintain their livelihoods, and 724 people sold their children as prostitutes. The people have complaints but no way to appeal, which is the extreme tragedy of life.

Threat to Pacific Security, Netherlands and Portugal Prepare for the Future, Intensify Naval Construction

Chicago News According to a London communication published in the Chicago Sunday Tribune, since Japan broke the London Naval Treaty and declared that after announcing the abolition of the Washington Treaty, it would build the navy it deemed necessary for its security in the Pacific, the relationship between the United States and Britain has been forced to become closer than ever before on Pacific affairs. In addition to Britain and the United States, Japan has also forced the Netherlands and Portugal to join the picture of the Pacific situation. The Netherlands and the two countries, which have not been regarded as important naval countries for generations, will now appear on the stage to maintain the white power in the Pacific. The Netherlands, at the beginning of Japan's invasion of the Pacific, was worried about the security of its Pacific colonies. Moreover, in Europe, it also felt that if one of Germany and France wanted to annex its territory, it would also be unable to defend itself. Therefore, its policy has always been to rely on a country without conflicts of interest, or a country with the same interests in the Pacific and Europe, that is, Britain.

Before the expiration of the Washington Treaty, Britain could not increase its navy, and Portugal was not a party to the Washington Treaty, so it was free to build warships. Portugal has now started building ships, which are built by British shipyards, and they are fast light cruisers, which are extremely suitable for the Far East archipelago. Is this a coincidence? However, the fact that these new ships will be used in the Pacific is an undisputed fact. After all, Portugal is also an important Pacific country, and it has at least the same reasons as the Netherlands to fear Japanese invasion. Therefore, it is now carrying out defensive works in Macau, and its plan includes a dock that can accommodate large ships that the Portuguese Navy does not currently have. (World News Agency)

British Eden and Air Minister Give Speeches on Security and Peace Reinforce Military Equipment to Prevent War

(London) Cabinet Minister Eden recently gave a speech in Warwickshire, saying, "Based on the experience we have gained, the arms race is not the way to build peace, but any country that feels insecure will inevitably reorganize its military. No one can stop it. As far as I know, there is only one way to security, that is, all countries clearly express their willingness to do their best to maintain international order, so that trust can be generated. My personal view of the collective deduction level system is like this, so I advocate that the United Kingdom must protect the League of Nations with all its strength, because the League of Nations is the only representative of collective peace." (15th, Havas telegram)

(London) Aviation Minister Sir Reesdale gave a speech in Chiddingstone, Medway district today, saying, "Preventing war with sufficient military force is the most effective method. Britain's expansion of its air force is to prevent war, not caused by panic. Regarding the maintenance of national security, the government has an unshirkable responsibility and will do its best. Moreover, it should go further and make efforts to establish a sky treaty to limit armaments, in order to maintain mutual security and general peace. But to achieve this goal, we must have sufficient military force and a strong military organization." (15th, Havas telegram)

Naval Issues: Anglo-German Talks Proceed Smoothly; Germany Submits Draft Shipbuilding Program; Italy and France's Replies Imminent

(Paris) The German delegation continued its meeting with British naval experts at the Admiralty today. They presented a draft of the German shipbuilding program, which is said to be entirely based on the American plan. The British plan, after any general compromise, can still be amended. Meanwhile, France is evidently anxious about the progress of the Anglo-German naval talks. Newspapers today stated that the British government is determined to tear up the naval clauses of the Treaty of Versailles without much hesitation, but France will never agree to Germany having a tonnage equal to 35% of British ships. (Reuters, 15th)

(London) British newspapers unanimously predict the success of the naval conference. It is reported that the British government has allowed Germany's request for 35%, and the talks are proceeding on this basis. Evening newspapers predict that the two sides can agree. The newspaper said that the German leader Hitler clearly understands the need for British naval superiority. If other continental countries increase their naval power, then Britain will naturally follow suit, and Germany, according to the Anglo-German agreement, can also increase proportionally. (National Telegram, 16th)

(London) The Anglo-German naval talks will continue from tomorrow, lasting about a week. An agreement in principle has been reached regarding the British request that a 25% ratio be applied to all classes of warships. However, it is generally believed that Britain is unwilling to take any binding action before clarifying the replies from the French and Italian governments. The replies from France and Italy are expected to arrive around Tuesday, and their content and wording will be the same. (Havas, 16th)

Content of Germany's Shipbuilding Plan

(London) It is rumored that Britain is about to ask France to send a delegation here to discuss the Anglo-German agreement on naval issues. This agreement has not yet been finalized, but Germany has reportedly promised not to build battleships of more than 35,000 tons. The country's naval shipbuilding plan includes five battleships, each with a displacement limited to 22,000 tons, with guns of 11 to 12 inches in caliber. The country will also follow the "Deutschland" class of pocket battleships and build six heavy cruisers of 8,000 or 10,000 tons, but the exact displacement of these warships has not yet been determined. In addition, it plans to build 36 destroyers of 1,000 tons, 18 submarines of 400 tons, and two aircraft carriers of 22,000 tons. Britain wants these to be completed gradually over a considerable number of years, so that the country can calmly replace its old warships. (Havas, 15th)

Anglo-German Naval Agreement Difficult for France to Accept

(Paris) The imminent conclusion of a naval agreement between Britain and Germany in London has caused widespread indignation here. Newspapers believe that the German naval tonnage being equal to 35% of the British navy is unacceptable to France. Le Petit Parisien said that Italy now intends to consult with France before submitting a reply to Britain, as the path it can follow must at least be perfectly aligned with France. The Socialist Party's newspaper Le Populaire also holds the same view. (Havas, 16th)

Avoiding Competition is Beneficial to Britain

(London) The Anglo-German naval agreement is likely to be successfully concluded. Because Germany bears a heavy burden of rearming its army and air force, building a navy at a rate of 35% compared to Britain would make it even more difficult to raise funds. It is unlikely to have extravagant hopes beyond this ratio. The British side believes that the Anglo-German naval agreement is practically beneficial in that: (1) Britain and Germany will not repeat the mistakes of before 1914 and engage in naval competition; (2) Germany recognizes that Britain's naval forces in the North Sea should be superior to Germany. In addition, the general situation can also be eased after the agreement is concluded, because Germany's military has fully restored its sovereignty and can participate in the collective security system, and the future naval conference is also expected to be held as scheduled. (Havas, 15th)

Army and Air Force Armaments Should Not Be Mixed

(London) France has raised objections to the Anglo-German naval agreement allowing Germany 35% of British tonnage, saying that if the Soviet Union increases its naval forces in the future, Germany may use this as an excuse to change this ratio. It also said that the principle of interdependence between army, navy, and air force armaments has been repeatedly proposed at disarmament conferences and seems applicable to naval issues, and that a treaty similar to the Locarno Treaty of the Skies could also be drawn up regarding naval issues. British naval figures have recently criticized this objection, saying that the 35% ratio is a fixed figure and there is no room for change. As for the principle of interdependence between army, navy, and air force armaments, it is not applicable to the navy, as the Washington Naval Treaty and the negotiations currently underway regarding the establishment of the Locarno Treaty of the Skies are two completely different matters and should not be confused. (Havas, 15th)

Turkey: National Defense Fundraising Campaign; Propaganda Lectures in Remote Areas; All Sectors of the Country Eagerly Donate

National defense propaganda is now spreading throughout the country. Whether in cities, towns, villages, or remote areas, there are daily lectures and gatherings of this kind, so that the general public knows the importance of national defense and the advantages and disadvantages of air warfare. In addition to propaganda, a national defense fundraising campaign has also been launched. It is reported that everyone from large stores to small farmers is enthusiastically donating. (National Telegram, 15th)

Belgium Several Belgian chemists are meeting in Liège, Belgium. As for what this poison gas is, we are still investigating, but we predict that if used in wartime, it will have extremely terrible effects. This poison gas emits a thick yellow smoke, and users must wear gas masks. In short, this incident proves that Germany is preparing for war." (Havas, 15th)

Tragedy of Nighttime Train Collision in London Suburbs: 15 Dead, 30 Injured

(London) A train collision occurred in Hertfordshire, England last night, killing fourteen people. According to eyewitnesses, a passenger express had just left the station and entered the main track when a mail express speeding from behind collided with the passenger train, resulting in the most tragic accident in Britain in several years. At the time, the passenger train's speed was about 20 miles per hour, while the mail train's speed was about 70 miles per hour, so the impact was extremely violent, and the passenger train was completely destroyed. Among the dead were five women and two young children. About 30 people were injured, with varying degrees of severity. Doctors and nurses rushed to help, but due to the darkness of the night, rescue was difficult. Although they worked overnight, the damaged vehicles were still blocking the tracks at 11 am this morning, so trains had to take a detour. (Reuters, 16th)

(London) In the train crash tragedy at Welwyn Garden City station last night, the death toll is 15, including five women and two children. Currently, 30 injured people are being treated in hospitals, some of whom are seriously injured and may be in danger of death. The accident site has been quickly inspected, and it is unlikely that more bodies will be found under the overturned carriages. In addition, about 100 people were injured or slightly injured. (Havas, 16th)

1935: Overseas German Nationals Exempt from Military Service; Joint Proclamation by Interior and Army Ministers

(Berlin) According to a joint proclamation issued by the Interior and Army Ministers, all German overseas nationals who are required to perform military service according to law will be exempted from doing so in 1935. (National Telegram, 15th)

Page 7

East Africa Could Go to War Any Day: Blockade of Suez Canal; British Public Opinion Leans Towards This; Italian Newspaper Responds with Convention

Recently, there has been a rumor that a certain country intends to block the Suez Canal at any time to prevent war in East Africa. This rumor is not worth refuting, because the Suez Canal is for international public use and is guaranteed by the Constantinople Convention of October 29, 1888. Italy also signed this convention. Article 1 states that the Suez Canal shall be freely accessible to merchant ships or warships of any country, whether in times of peace or war. Therefore, there is no reason to block this canal under international law. This provision cannot be unilaterally changed by any country. If such a threat occurs, according to Article 8 of the convention, this issue should also be submitted to the signatory countries for joint discussion. (National Telegram, 15th)

Anglo-Egyptian Talks: Three Questions Raised

Milan According to reports in this newspaper, Egyptian Prime Minister Nassim Pasha and British High Commissioner to Egypt Lampson spoke, believing that the Italo-Ethiopian war would inevitably harm Egypt's interests. Therefore, Nassim Pasha raised the following questions to Lampson: If the Italo-Ethiopian war breaks out, what measures will Britain take to prevent it? Can Britain prevent Italian aircraft from crossing Egyptian territory? Can Britain block the Suez Canal to prevent Italian warships from entering and leaving? Can Britain assist Egypt and the Lake Tana region of Abyssinia, which obtains water from the Nile? (National Telegram, 15th)

British Newspapers Advocate: Invoking the League of Nations Covenant

Regarding the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia, some British newspapers have proposed that if Italy and Abyssinia go to war, Britain should invoke Article 20 of the League of Nations Covenant to blockade the Suez Canal as a means of sanctioning Italy. (Note: Article 20, Paragraph 2 of the League of Nations Covenant states that if a member of the League has obligations undertaken before joining the League that conflict with the articles of the Covenant, it shall immediately take steps to be freed from these obligations.) The Italian newspaper Il Popolo d'Italia recently discussed this issue and responded, saying, "If the Suez Canal, and by extension, all straits and navigable waterways, can be used as a tool for the League of Nations to sanction member states, just as an international air force should be used as a tool for sanctions, then the current straits system must be substantially revised and replaced with a new system, endowed with an international character, and the privileges currently enjoyed by certain countries must be abolished." (Note: Turkey's request to remilitarize the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits is most opposed by Britain. This statement in the Italian newspaper is probably referring to this.) (Havas, 15th)

On the Italo-Ethiopian Dispute: The British Government's Attitude; The League of Nations Cannot Be Relied Upon; The Manchurian Incident Serves as a Warning; Unwilling to Hurt the Mouse for Fear of Breaking the Vase, Driving Italy into Germany's Arms; Sir Samuel Hoare's Diplomacy is Gentle, Still Intending to Act as a Mediator

The British attitude towards the Abyssinian issue should be studied from two aspects: one is the relationship with the League of Nations, and the other is the relationship with the interests of Abyssinia and Britain itself. From the perspective of the League of Nations, Britain has always believed that since Abyssinia is a member state of the League of Nations, it should enjoy all the rights of the League of Nations enjoyed by other member states, and that receiving assistance from other member states when its territory is invaded is also one of its rights. Therefore, when the Emperor of Abyssinia applied to the League of Nations on May 20 to resolve the Walwal incident and delineate the Italo-Ethiopian border through peaceful means, Britain made every effort to avoid war and endeavored to promote the organization of an arbitration committee to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. Indeed, due to the firm attitude of the British representative Eden, Italy finally accepted the resolution of the League of Nations Administrative Council on May 25. Afterwards, Eden returned to his country, and the newspapers praised him greatly, saying that Eden was the reason for the League of Nations' victory in resolving the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. As a result, Eden's hopes of becoming Foreign Secretary steadily increased. Unexpectedly, the cabinet was reorganized on June 9, and the post of Foreign Secretary was given to the Secretary of State for India, Sir Samuel Hoare. One reason for this was that Eden was too young, but in the observation of political figures, it was said that Eden's overly tough attitude in the Italo-Ethiopian dispute was also a major reason why he could not succeed as Foreign Secretary. Recently, incidents have occurred again on the border between Italian territory and Abyssinia, and Italy has once again spoken eloquently, saying that it must take new measures to avoid creating a new situation. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini also delivered a speech, saying that "Italy has the need to solve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute on its own and will not be concerned about anything." It can be seen that Italy's attitude is very clear. The governments of various European countries know that if they still use the League of Nations as a shield to prevent Italy from taking action against Abyssinia, then Italy will certainly retaliate by withdrawing from the League. Subsequently, Italian newspapers criticized Britain with fierce rhetoric, and the Italian government vaguely revealed its intention to approach Berlin. Under these circumstances, the British government knows that if it invokes Articles 15 and 16 of the League of Nations Covenant to impose sanctions on Italy, the League of Nations will be facing a second Manchurian Incident, and the one emulating Japan will be a European country, so the situation will be more serious than the Manchurian Incident. As a result, Italy and Germany may compromise with each other, divide Austria, and completely change the European diplomatic situation, and a group opposed to the League of Nations will be established, and there is no danger greater than this. British political figures therefore observed that the policy of the new Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare must be more gentle. The recent sudden cessation of attacks on Britain by Italian newspapers must be related to Sir Samuel Hoare's gentle diplomacy. In addition, there is another matter that is quite noteworthy. Recently, it has been reported that the United Kingdom, France and Italy, signatories to the 1906 Abyssinia Treaty, will act jointly to transfer Abyssinia's important economic rights to Italy and build railways in Abyssinian territory to connect with the Italian territory of Somaliland as a condition for Italy to stop military action. This tentative proposal was issued by London. Although the Italian government denied it, it did not absolutely reject it. From this, it can be seen that it is not impossible for the United Kingdom, France and Italy to conduct secret negotiations with Abyssinia soon to satisfy Italy. Re-examine Britain's own interests. Britain has significant interests in the interior of Anglo-Egyptian Sudan based on various treaties prior to 1906, and there is no reason to give up these. Later, the United Kingdom, France and Italy concluded the 1906 Abyssinia Treaty, which divided Abyssinia into spheres of influence and mutually recognized each other. Although France abandoned this right, the United Kingdom and Italy did not. Britain's main interest lies in the famous Lake Tana. After the water level of the lake is raised, it can be used to irrigate most of the farmland in Anglo-Egyptian Sudan, so as to grow cotton and supply the British industry. Currently, the construction of embankments around Lake Tana is underway. The committee organized by Sudan, Egypt and Abyssinia is currently discussing the details of the water distribution of the Blue Nile. London believes that this water conservancy project is based on past contracts and has nothing to do with the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, and does not harm Italy's interests, so it is very strange that Italian newspapers attack this matter. In general, in the coming months, Britain will continue to act as a mediator to eliminate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute and continue to persuade Italy not to engage in war. However, if war unfortunately breaks out, Britain will probably not take any action, because Britain does not want to hurt the mouse for fear of breaking the vase, so as to drive Italy into Germany's arms. If Britain intends to take action on the Italo-Ethiopian war, the only way is to blockade the Suez Canal. The Suez Canal was subject to a treaty concluded by various countries in 1888, which stipulates that ships of all countries should be allowed to pass freely in peacetime or wartime. However, British Liberal Party member of parliament Yude published a declaration in the Lower House on June 7, advocating invoking Article 20 of the League of Nations Covenant (which stipulates that member states should take steps to repeal international obligations undertaken before joining the League of Nations that conflict with the articles of the Covenant) to abolish the system of free navigation of the Suez Canal in wartime. Mandel's proposal may be a way to deal with Italy, but in practice, it is difficult to implement. (Havas, 15th)

Saturday Set as Fascist Movement Day: Full Focus on Military Training

The Cabinet, in accordance with Mussolini's wishes, has stipulated that Saturday afternoon be Fascist Movement Day. All work by the people must cease, and they must devote all their energy to military training and physical exercise. According to the existing regulations of Fascist groups in Italy, Sunday is reserved for personal rest and cultivation. However, the current regulation extends this practice to all people. According to the Cabinet's order, all work must stop at one o'clock on Saturday afternoon, and employers must not deduct wages. If employers are only willing to pay half wages, then the amount of work during the week must be reduced. (National Telegram, 15th)

Stratosphere Flight: Upson Again Fails; Engine Encountered Obstacles Mid-Flight; Forced to Land in Wichita

California White Burbank Famous American aviator Captain Albert William Stevens' attempt to fly from California across the stratosphere to New York has failed again. Mr. Stevens put on an "oxygen suit" today and set off in a plane, intending to fly to New York at an altitude of 33,000 feet in seven or eight hours. However, he only flew as far as Davenport, Iowa. At that time, he noticed that the engine was encountering obstacles, so he hurriedly flew back and landed in Wichita, Kansas. This was Mr. Stevens' fourth experiment in stratosphere flight. Its purpose is to explore the possibility of using the stratosphere as a medium for scheduled commercial air transport. (Reuters, 15th)

Aftermath of Luo Binghui's Remnants Disturbing the Zhejiang Border

Hangzhou Communication: The southeastern border of Zhejiang Province adjoins the three provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian. The two bandit leaders, Fang Zhimin and Luo Binghui, had entrenched themselves in eastern Jiangxi for six or seven years, causing harm to the local area. Last year, they attempted to implement their plan to expand the bandit area, disturbing more than ten counties including Jiangshan, Changshan, Kaihua, Quzhou, Longyou, Shou, Jingning, and Qingyuan along the Anhui-Zhejiang border. After the Zhejiang Security Regiment led by Hui Jishi, together with the National Army, launched a campaign to suppress them, the key figures Fang Zhimin, Liu Chouxi, Xun Weizhou, and others were captured and killed, and the main bandit forces were gradually eliminated. The border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui gained temporary peace. At that time, although eastern Jiangxi was declared cleared, the bandit forces on the Fujian border were not yet eliminated. All the remnants of Luo Binghui's forces gathered in the southern Fujian area. Recently, Luo Binghui's puppet independent division commander, Su Yu, and Luo Binghui's puppet army group chief of staff, Liu Ying, joined forces in southern Fujian, with a force of more than 2,000 men and complete weaponry. They have also gathered the remnants of Fang Zhimin's bandits and are roaming through the counties bordering Fujian and Zhejiang provinces. The southeastern Zhejiang areas of Jinhua, Quzhou, Yanping, Wenzhou, and Chuzhou have all been disturbed, with incidents of kidnapping, burning, robbery, and murder, causing considerable damage to the local area. Fortunately, the Security Regiment quickly pursued and suppressed them. The bandits did not dare to stay long in any one place they passed through and immediately moved to other places. The details of the suppression and defense are as follows: In early April of this year, Su Yu and Liu Ying joined forces and infiltrated Qingyuan County on the Zhejiang border from Zhenhe County on the Fujian border. They immediately broke into smaller units and scattered to loot, increasing the number of targets for our bandit suppression troops and making it difficult to advance. They disturbed the counties of Qingyuan, Jingning, and Taishun in mid-April, always returning to their base in Zhenhe, Songxi, and Shouning in Fujian. The Zhejiang Security Regiment and the regular forces and core teams of various counties pursued and intercepted them day and night. Although some annihilation and captures occurred at Liushantou and Taoyang in Jingning, on the border of Songxi and Qingyuan, and at Meikeng and Gejiadishangbiao, the loss to the main bandit force was limited. Because the bandit force was purely mobile in nature, using the narrow paths of the border counties, and immediately retreated back to their nest on the Fujian border upon encountering interception. On April 30, Su Yu and Liu Ying's combined force of more than 600 men and guns re-entered the Qilang Village from Qingyuan Hahu, hoping to rely on the dangerous terrain for defense. At that time, two regiments from the National Army's Liu Brigade joined the siege, sealing off their escape route. The bandits then fled north to Yixi Village in Longquan, and after our troops pursued them separately, the bandits turned south to Bodailling in Longquan between Huangcun and Yecun, and溃入松溪in Songxi in Fujian via the northwest of Qingyuan. On May 7, they split into two groups, each with about two or three hundred men, and after successive blockades, one group retreated back to Shouning, and the other group fled to the border of Longyou, Suichang, and Songxi, turning into Daxi in Suichang, planning to flee to Jiangshan Dingcun. After being severely suppressed head-on, they retreated to the border between Jiangshan and Pucheng. On the 14th, more than 800 bandits were discovered again, attempting to flee to Longqing. After being blocked, a portion fled into Longquan, and after pursuit, they fled through Cai'ao Ridge to Guanju. A portion of the bandits who retreated to Pucheng on the 18th re-entered Suichang Dazhe to Songyang Gushi. At that time, the Tax Police Regiment also received orders to join the suppression. The bandits were attacked and fled to Damafu in Suichang, reaching Zhangcun in the northeast, in an extremely difficult situation. They then crossed to Tangxi, fled through Dongkeng to Shangyang Village on the border of Tangxi Longyou. After being blocked by the government army, they fled again through the area of Xikou Lingshan Temple Xiashibidi in Longyou, planning to flee to Hushan Town in Suichang. At that time, a portion of the bandits were only thirty li away from Nuzhou Quanwang in Qu County. Our army gathered from all sides to pursue them, and the bandits split into groups and fled to places such as Lutou Huduikou on the border of Longyou, Suichang, and Jiangshan, where many were killed along the way. The bandits then split into small groups and fled to Wangwu, Huangshayao, and Yinling Xuanping County. On the 30th, the bandit groups reunited again and fled southeast from the vicinity of Tangxi. The bandits southwest of Suichang fled to Wushankou again, disintegrated and scattered, and roamed through the counties of Xuanping, Suichang, Longyou, Longquan, Jingning, Songyang, Tangxi, Wuyi, Taishun, and Qingyuan. At that time, various groups such as Fan Chumin and Huang Ligui took the opportunity to infiltrate Zhejiang, echoing each other, taking advantage of the rugged mountain roads on the border and the inconvenience of transportation. They fled hither and thither, like wolves running amok. All the blocking and suppression troops are still pursuing them day and night. In the battle of Beijie Town on the 10th of this month, more than 300 bandits were completely annihilated, and many others were captured. Currently, the Zhejiang provincial authorities have drafted a concrete plan to eliminate the roving bandits, which will be submitted for approval and implementation immediately, and have telegraphed to the garrison in southern Fujian for joint blocking to cut off the bandits' return route. Then, the bandits who are like roving bandits can be eliminated in a short period of time. (June 16)

Yu Xuezhong's Troops Pass Through Baoding for Shaanxi Successively, Guan Linzheng's Troops Also Head to Northern Shaanxi to Suppress Bandits, Population Increase After Hebei Provincial Government Moved to Baoding

Baoding Communication: The former Chairman of Hebei Province, Yu Xuezhong, has been ordered to serve as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the border area of Sichuan, Gansu, and Shaanxi provinces. Yu has decided to first transfer the three divisions of Li Zhentang, Du Jiwu, and Chen Guanqun to the west. Li's troops arrived in Baoding at 4:00 PM on the 12th, taking two special trains. The headquarters of the 51st Army stationed here dispatched personnel to the station to take care of everything. The first train consisted of eight covered cars and thirteen open cars, and the second train consisted of seven covered cars and thirteen open cars. The 3rd Battalion of the Division, as well as the military supply and ordnance departments, arrived here on these two trains. The first train departed for Zhengzhou at 5:10 PM and will transfer to the Longhai Line to the west. The second train is also scheduled to depart that night. It is reported that the railway bureau has prepared a total of ten train cars to facilitate the aforementioned transfers. Chen Guanqun's troops are now concentrated in a certain location, and Du Jiwu's troops are also preparing to move. Their artillery brigade and cavalry division are scheduled to depart last. The army headquarters has decided that all troops will be completely transferred within five days. Yu Xuezhong returned to Baoding from Pingjin a few days ago, and various circles went to the station to welcome him. After Yu got off the train, he immediately summoned officers above the rank of lieutenant to give instructions, reporting on the relocation of the troops. After the instructions, he went to his private residence to rest. In the afternoon, the heads of various departments visited. Yu is scheduled to go to Zhengzhou on the 13th to coordinate the movement of the troops. He plans to stay in Zhengzhou for a short period of time and then lead the troops into Shaanxi when the headquarters of the 51st Army arrives in Zhengzhou. The vanguard of the 25th Division of Guan Linzheng's troops passed through Baoding and went south in the afternoon of the 12th and will go to northern Shaanxi to suppress bandits via the Zhengtai Railway. Also, the 4th Brigade of the 2nd Division of Huang Jie's troops arrived in Baoding on foot from Pingjin yesterday and went south in the afternoon. The remaining troops in Baoding are also scheduled to depart south on the 13th. Huang himself arrived in Baoding from Pingjin at 4:00 PM on the 13th.

According to a recent investigation by the Public Security Bureau, the population of Baoding is over 80,000 in the urban area, mostly engaged in commerce. According to an investigation by the Qingyuan County government in the rural area, it is about 400,000 people, mostly engaged in agriculture. There are only a few foreign missionaries and a Japanese merchant named Miyazaki. It is learned that after the provincial government moved here, the population of the urban area has increased by about 4,000, according to estimates by the Public Security Bureau. (14th)

Chaoshan Holds Security Conference, Most Communist Bandits in Various Districts Eliminated

Shantou Communication: The remaining bandits on the Fujian-Jiangxi border have been gradually eliminated. Chen Jitang previously sent Chief of Staff Miao Peinan to the east to discuss with the military officers stationed in Chaozhou and Meizhou about measures to maintain stability and suppress bandits within the territory. Li Yangjing, the commissioner of the Eastern District and commander of the Third Army, has also been touring the Eastern District from the province recently and has now arrived in Huiyang and will soon arrive in Shantou. The Eastern District Commissioner's Office telegraphed an order summoning the magistrates and the deputy directors of the security team training from the 24 counties in the Eastern District to arrive in Shantou before the 17th to attend the security conference and to inspect the military and police in various counties. Currently, the military forces stationed in Chaozhou and Meizhou include the troops of Huang Renbao, Huang Yanzhen, and Deng Longguang. The banditry in the eastern territory of Dabu on the Fujian border has been slightly suppressed. The remnants of Zhang Dingcheng's forces, numbering over 1,000, in the Phoenix Mountains have been surrounded and suppressed by Zeng Youren's brigade, resulting in the deaths of over 500 bandits. The bandits fled back to the mountains of Yongding and Pinghe on the Fujian border. Zeng's brigade is currently stationed in Raoping City, striving to search and suppress the remaining bandits in Phoenix Mountains. The remaining bandits in Sangpu Mountain, Beishan, Nanshan, and Baxiang Mountain are also being diligently searched for by the military and police. Huang Tianping, the bandit leader of Sangpu Mountain, secretly returned to Zhaopu Township in Fujian last week and was reported to the defense army by the district chief, who killed Huang. Also, troops stationed in Jiaoshan Township entered Tianxin Township in Sangpu Mountain and captured a male and a female bandit. Various districts and townships near the mountain are actively engaged in joint defense. Chen Yubo, the deputy district chief of the 9th District of Chaoyang, was captured and shot by Deng Longguang for extorting the local people to provide supplies to the local bandits in Nanshan. The bandits in Nanshan have been surrounded by Deng's division for two months, resulting in the deaths of over 500 bandits and the discovery of eight important bandit organizations, including prisons. More than 120 men and women hostages were rescued. Recently, Battalion Commander Liu of the Huilai defense army led troops to Dagutan in Nanshan, where they uncovered one sham political prison and one capitalist prison. These prisons were located in stone caves. When the defense army arrived, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. The defense army finally dispersed the bandits. The remaining bandits, numbering over twenty, hid in the depths of the stone cave. Battalion Commander Liu led a hand-picked team to rush into the cave, killing on the spot A Lei, the head of the Nanshan fake military affairs department, and more than ten key bandits, capturing ten male and female bandits, seizing more than ten long and short guns, and rescuing twelve hostages. It is reported that the bandits' fake military headquarters is located near Dawo Mountain. Battalion Commander Liu rushed to encircle and suppress again, killing more than ten bandits, capturing ten guns, and taking five prisoners. Because the fake military headquarters was set on the waist of a precipitous cliff, with stone caves inside, making it difficult to climb, many bandits escaped. Generally speaking, most of the major communist bandits in Chaozhou and Meizhou have been eliminated through the joint suppression of various armies and are no longer capable.

Li Yangjing inspected the military in Chaozhou and Jiangdong and paid close attention to the work of training security teams and reserve teams in various counties. This is a necessary stage for implementing conscription. Currently, the police teams in various counties in Chaozhou and Meizhou are organized and trained in imitation of the Guangxi province. Starting from August this year, the money and grain in various counties will be changed to land tax, calculated according to the measured and investigated tax amount of land, which can collect 14 million yuan annually. The Finance Department stipulates that half of it will be retained by the counties as administrative and security expenses, so there will be more than 7 million yuan of security expenses each year. Li Yangjing came to Chaoshan to inspect the military and convene a security conference, which is probably related to this matter.

Overseas Chinese Representatives from Siam Return to Guangdong to Urge Speedy Treaty Negotiation and Abolition of Harsh Regulations

Shantou Communication: The maltreatment of overseas Chinese in Siam has aroused a nationwide call for a boycott of Siamese rice. As a result, the Siamese government is quite willing to change its ways. The Overseas Chinese Club of Bangkok in Siam convened a general meeting of overseas Chinese organizations and elected Zheng Haonan and Li Fubiao to return to the country to make a sincere appeal to the authorities, urging them to quickly conclude a commercial treaty and abolish the harsh regulations. Zheng and Li passed through Shantou yesterday on their way to the province. According to them, the latest situation of anti-Chinese activities in Siam is as follows: (1) Each ship sailing from China to Siam shall not allow more than 500 Chinese immigrants to enter. (2) New immigrants to Siam must pay an entrance tax of 100 baht, which is about 160 silver dollars, at one time. (3) Uneducated women are not allowed to disembark under any circumstances, otherwise the original ship will be escorted back. (4) Overseas Chinese laborers' children under the age of seven must pay a deposit of 500 baht when leaving the country. If the person is over eighteen years old and does not return to Siam, the deposit will be confiscated. (5) Overseas Chinese laborers' children who are eighteen years old have the obligation to serve in the military. (6) The Overseas Chinese Business Regulations previously promulgated stipulate that the bookkeeping used by Chinese stores must be changed to Siamese, and Siamese must be hired as clerks, which must be implemented as soon as possible. (7) Overseas Chinese are not allowed to gather for resistance meetings, otherwise they will be punished with extreme penalties for violating national law. (8) After Siam closed overseas Chinese schools this spring, all overseas Chinese children were forcibly transferred to Thai schools, and the original Chinese schools were virtually eliminated. (9) Restrictions on remittances by overseas Chinese to their home country. (10) Overseas Chinese returning to the country must obtain an exit paper from the Siamese government and are restricted from carrying more than 100 yuan in cash out of the country. (11) Promulgation of the number of Chinese laborers to be employed and the time of service. (12) For fishing boats operated by Chinese, each ship owner must hire a Siamese person to serve as the captain, and Siamese persons must also account for one-tenth of the fishing crew, otherwise they will not be allowed to go fishing. According to Zheng and Li, 3 million overseas Chinese, under this severe oppression, have no other way but to appeal to the government for help. At present, overseas Chinese commerce and industry have been greatly damaged, and the fear of unemployment is becoming more and more serious. Since May, one million people have returned to their country due to being unable to bear the oppression. Therefore, the local overseas Chinese elected Zheng and Li to return to their country to earnestly ask for government assistance. (12th)

Songjiang: Joy of Sweet Rain, Passerby Dies

It is the season of mold, but there has been a long drought. The rice seedlings are withering. On the 16th, the weather was scorching hot. By noon, dark clouds were dense, and sweet rain was celebrated. However, around 4:00 PM, when the fourth-class train from Hangzhou arrived in Songjiang, a passenger got off the train. While walking south of the Malu Bridge, he suddenly encountered a torrential downpour. He ran as fast as he could, but accidentally stumbled and fell to the ground and died immediately. Passersby stopped to watch. Someone recognized the deceased as Chen Shaohong from Shihudang, who worked as a farmer. His sister currently lives in the Zhu residence near Foyu Bridge in the city. The deceased was wearing a black cloth jacket and white cloth pants. The patrol officer immediately reported the incident to the Public Security Substation. His sister was summoned to the scene to identify the body. She was very grieved. The Songjiang Public Security Bureau has requested the County Court to send someone to examine the body.

Jiading: Student Police Arrests Ship Crew Members, Dispute

On the 14th, at 11:00 AM, the connecting ship between Jiading and Nanxiang on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway departed from Jiading. A student police officer surnamed Wu from the Nanxiang Public Security Sub-bureau boarded the ship to Nanxiang. Sheng Guisheng, a crew member, asked him to buy a ticket. Wu initially refused but then agreed to buy a half-price ticket. Sheng insisted on a full-price ticket in accordance with the regulations. Passengers on the ship also spoke in support. Wu reluctantly bought a full-price ticket. Unexpectedly, he considered this an insult. After arriving in Nanxiang, he did not hand over the purchased ticket to the ticket collector and reported the incident to the Public Security Sub-bureau of the town by telephone. As a result, dozens of student police officers came to make trouble for Sheng. However, Sheng had already supervised the ship north to Jiading. The police officers waited at the dock. Someone, fearing trouble, telegraphed the Jiading Shipping Company. The company considered there were passengers with Shanghai-Nanjing train connecting tickets waiting in Nanxiang. So, not avoiding danger, it still sailed to Nanxiang at 3:00 PM. When it arrived at the dock, the police officers immediately arrested Sheng Guisheng and the other nine crew members and took them to the bureau. The bureau chief, Zheng Qi, interrogated them and ordered them to be detained together. The crew members were detained, and the ship could not sail. The passengers waiting for the ship made a great commotion. The chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Zhixiao, and the executive member of the county, Lu Linxun, heard the news and went to the bureau to request their temporary release, but Zheng refused. The shipping company urgently sent an employee, Qi Wenzhen, to Nanxiang with money to return the money for the connecting tickets and take them back. The passengers then dispersed. When the county's Public Security Bureau Chief, Chen Youmin, heard the news, he ordered the sub-bureau chief Zheng to release the detained crew members. It was already midnight. On the 15th, the crew members went on strike and the ship stopped running. The matter is currently under negotiation.

Wuxi: Joint Meeting of Chamber of Commerce Executives and Supervisors

Yesterday, the local county Chamber of Commerce held its fourteenth joint meeting of executives and supervisors, chaired by Qian Sunqing. The following important items were resolved: (1) The Education Promotion Association sent a letter requesting cooperation in establishing a vocational supplementary school and attached a draft plan. The matter requires fundraising, but the market is currently depressed and the financial situation is extremely panic. It was decided to send a letter of reply immediately, and to consider social economy and negotiate the matter when the market turns slightly. (2) The Jiangsu Finance Department and the Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation successively sent letters informing of the organization of a commodity marketing organization in the province. It was decided to follow the results of the meeting held in the province on the 3rd of this month and first have the Finance Department hire bankers and businessmen to establish a design committee, and then wait for the provincial department's design before contacting them for handling.

Changshu: Matricide Case, Inspection Conducted in Township

Xu Jinfu, an unnatural son of the Huanpu Township in Luyuan, whose animal instincts flared up the day before, actually used a kitchen knife and a sickle to cut and kill his own mother, Qian. The situation was recorded in yesterday's newspaper. On the 15th, the county government's trial investigator, Hu Cheng, accompanied by the coroner Shen Guifang, went to the township to inspect the case. Because it was an unprecedented major case of unnatural incest, the countryside paid extraordinary attention. No less than three thousand people went to the scene to inspect the body. The murderer, Xu Jinfu, was taken to the scene by the Public Security Bureau to await trial. At 4:30, the inspection began. It was found that there were eight knife wounds on the back of the deceased's head, neck, chest, and other parts, and the throat was cut, which was indeed fatal. After the inspection, the judge returned to the city by the original ship, which was already past 10:00 PM. The murderer is still being taken back by the Public Security Bureau and will be handed over to the county's judiciary for interrogation on the 16th.

Yangzhou: First District Joint Examination Held in Yangzhou

The high school graduation joint examination for this province's 23rd year is divided into eight districts. This county is designated as the first district, with the Provincial Yangzhou High School as the first district's joint examination venue. The joint examination is scheduled to be held from June 19th to 22nd. In addition to the fact that the Education Department sent a chief examiner to Yangzhou to preside over the joint examination, yesterday it specially instructed Xin Fang, the director of the county's Education Bureau, to be the proctor to assist in the handling.

Nantong: Discussing Relief for Drought in Four Townships

The Tongyi has not rained for a long time, and the rivers in the four townships have dried up to the bottom. Cotton and rice are short of irrigation water and have withered. At present, drinking water is lacking. The locals are digging springs at the bottom of the river. The Construction Bureau is trying to alleviate the drought by introducing Jiang tidal irrigation and is planning to use electric pumps at the port to draw water.

Jiashan: Kidnapping Case in Coral Village

Qi Qichang, a resident of Coral Village at the junction of Yu Hui and Dingzha, is wealthy and cultivates more than 200 acres of land, but the area is frequented by bandits. Therefore, Qichang himself and others, such as Jin Zheng, moved elsewhere to avoid them. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 15th, someone knocked on the door of the Qi family. The workers, not being careful, immediately put on their clothes and opened the door. More than a dozen bandits rushed in, tied up all the workers, and forbade them from making noise. They broke into the room. At that time, Qi's wife was holding her only eight-month-old boy, intending to find a place to hide. They were spotted by the bandits, who stopped Qi's wife and snatched the boy from her arms. They scattered with whoops. Also, on the afternoon of the 15th, more than 300 refugees from Hunan suddenly arrived at the Tianrenzhuangzhen Rindianbang and acted recklessly, looting the entire village. No one was spared, especially the Shoulin family in the suburbs suffered the greatest losses.

Hangzhou: Fujian-Jiangxi Railway Begins Survey

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway organized a Fujian-Jiangxi Railway survey team and appointed Wang Xiuqin as the team leader. Now, with the passports for Fujian and Jiangxi having been obtained, the team left Qu County on the 16th, arrived in Shangrao, entered Fujian, and began the survey work. It is expected to be completed in about a month.
