Local News

Representatives from All Circles Held a Memorial Meeting Yesterday Morning for the Premier's Guangzhou Assassination Attempt; Chairman Wu Xingya Reported on the Events

According to the Kuomintang News Agency, yesterday (the 16th) was the anniversary of the Premier's Guangzhou assassination attempt. The Municipal Party Headquarters specially convened representatives from all circles of the city at 9:00 AM yesterday in the headquarters' auditorium to hold a memorial meeting. Committee Member Wu Xingya presided over the meeting, Du Mengsen served as recorder, and Zhang Hanyun served as master of ceremonies. The Municipal Public Security Bureau and the police departments of the two concessions implemented security measures to prevent reactionary elements from disrupting public order. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives:

Wu Xingya from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Qiu Yunming from the Land Bureau, Wang Zongjian from the Jianghai Customs Superintendent Office, Gao Wuhe from the First Special District Court, Dong Chongshan from the Second Branch of the High Court, Liu Cuping from the Ordnance Factory Storage Office, Yang Dean from the New Life Movement Association, Ye Xianggao from the General Labor Union, Lin Kecong from the Municipal Women's Association, Qiu Jialiang from the First Special District Citizens' Association, Huang Xianggu from the Second Special District Citizens' Association, Du Mengsen from the Cooperative Enterprise Promotion Association, Yu Yaoqiu from the Baoshan Fellow-Villagers Association, and representatives from the First District Paper Makers Union, Umbrella Union, Dried Goods Union, Pharmaceutical Union, and various agencies, organizations, and schools, totaling over 160 people.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Wu Xingya, Recorder Du Mengsen, Master of Ceremonies Zhang Hanyun. After the customary ceremonies, the Chairman reported on the Premier's assassination attempt in Guangzhou thirteen years ago, dividing his speech into three sections. The first section concerned the long-term and immediate causes of Chen Jiongming's rebellion and his intentions. The second section described the detailed circumstances and all the events surrounding the Premier's assassination attempt. The third section described the Premier's magnanimity and composure in the face of danger, emphasizing the significance of his selfless spirit as a model for us to emulate. Because Committee Member Wu was present at the time, his report was very detailed. The original speech was too long and is omitted.

Meeting Slogans

(1) Inherit the Premier's revolutionary spirit; (2) Accomplish the Premier's unfinished legacy; (3) Eliminate the Red Bandits; (4) Eliminate corrupt and inferior officials; (5) Complete local autonomy; (6) Strive for productive construction; (7) Revive the Chinese nation; (8) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (9) Long live the Republic of China.

Implementation of Security

Because yesterday was a revolutionary memorial day, the Municipal Public Security Bureau specially ordered each branch bureau and police station to increase the number of stationed police and patrol police for strict security. Simultaneously, inspectors, detectives, and male and female inspectors were dispatched in separate groups, together with stationed police, to inspect pedestrians. Special attention was given to the vicinity of schools and factories. The authorities of the two concessions also separately ordered their respective police stations to be especially vigilant, it was said.

The Coffin of Martyr Liao Zhongkai Arrived in Shanghai Today and Will Proceed to Beijing Tomorrow Morning; The Municipal Party Headquarters Issued a Message to Comrades and Compatriots; Radio Broadcast Reporting Liao's Revolutionary History; A Public Memorial Service Will Be Held in the City Tomorrow Morning at 7:00 AM

According to the Kuomintang News Agency, the special ship carrying the coffin of martyr Liao Zhongkai arrived in Shanghai at 6:30 AM today, docking at the China Merchants Central Wharf in Yangshupu. The special envoy sent by the Central Government to welcome the coffin, Central Committee Member Chen Shuren, as well as Mayor Wu, committee members of the Municipal Party Headquarters, bureau chiefs, representatives from various agencies and organizations, and Boy Scouts, all went to the wharf to welcome it. The Army Officer School specially dispatched Liu Qian to Shanghai as a representative of all officers and students to welcome the coffin, expressing their respect.

Strict Security Along the Wharf Route

The special coffin-welcoming ship docked at the China Merchants Bureau wharf. Due to the large number of people welcoming the coffin, the party and government agencies, in order to protect safety, specially notified the Public Works Department through the Municipal Government, requesting the Police Department to be vigilant. At the same time, the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched many detectives to the wharf and along the route for security and protection.

Public Memorial Service Tomorrow Morning at 7:00 AM

Tomorrow morning at 7:00 AM, the city will hold a public memorial service led by the party and government agencies, with Mayor Wu and standing committee members of the Municipal Party Headquarters Wu Kaixian, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Tong Xingbai, and others presiding over the ceremony. Heads of various agencies and leaders of various organizations throughout the city will all participate in the memorial service. After the ceremony, the hearse will be attached to the 8:00 AM express train to proceed to Beijing.

Radio Broadcast Reporting Liao's History

In addition to jointly issuing a notice with the Municipal Government to all circles, sending representatives to participate in the coffin-welcoming public memorial service, and issuing a message to comrades and compatriots, the Municipal Party Headquarters ordered the Municipal Privately-Run Broadcasting Wireless Electricity Industry Association to instruct all radio stations in the city to broadcast sound on these two days, today and tomorrow, reporting on the history of Martyr Liao's involvement in the revolutionary cause, in order to promote the spirit of struggle of revolutionary martyrs for citizens to emulate.

Municipal Party Headquarters' Message to Comrades and Compatriots

The Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Municipal Party Headquarters in this city specially issued a message to comrades and compatriots regarding the passage of Mr. Liao Zhongkai's coffin through Shanghai. The original text is as follows: "Dear comrades and compatriots, the Central Government has specially dispatched an envoy to Guangdong to welcome and bury Mr. Liao Zhongkai's coffin beside the Premier's mausoleum. Now, on the day of its passage through Shanghai and the temporary placement of the coffin, in addition to devoutly holding a memorial service, we would like to briefly describe the historical facts of Mr. Liao's revolution and his great spirit as follows, to inform comrades and compatriots. Mr. Liao, named Enxu, styled Zhongkai, was a native of Huiyang County, Guangdong. His father was a merchant in America. Mr. Liao was born on March 10th, thirty-four years before the founding of the Republic of China. At the age of seventeen, he returned to China. At the age of twenty-two, he married Madam He Xiangning, and they were a devoted couple. Subsequently, he went to Japan to study economics and finance, achieving profound accomplishments. When the Russo-Japanese War broke out and China was in danger, the Premier went to Tokyo, gathered revolutionary comrades from seventeen provinces, and organized the Chinese Tongmenghui. Mr. Liao and his wife both joined. Later, during the Xinhai Revolution, the campaign to punish Yuan Shikai, and the protection of the Constitution, he participated in every battle. In particular, in managing finance, he provided great assistance to the revolutionary military needs. In peacetime, he especially strived to promote the peasant and worker movements and improve the lives of peasants and workers. Mr. Liao also contributed greatly to the establishment of the Whampoa Military Academy. After the Premier's death, Mr. Liao assisted Comrade Chiang Kai-shek in suppressing the Yang and Liu rebellions and assisted in organizing the National Government, unifying military and civilian finances to consolidate the revolutionary foundation. Mr. Liao loved the party as his life and hated evil as his enemy. Consequently, counter-revolutionaries conspired against Mr. Liao. On August 20th of the fourteenth year, Mr. Liao was assassinated by counter-revolutionaries, at the young age of forty-nine. This is not only a major loss for our party, but also a major loss for the entire nation. Mr. Liao's noble character, outstanding achievements, and profound knowledge are well known to the world. It must be known that Mr. Liao's achievements were so great because they were based on the cultivation of his revolutionary personality. Today, as we welcome and bury Mr. Liao, we dare to present several points as models: (1) Perseverance: Mr. Liao followed the Premier and devoted himself to the revolution for more than twenty years. During that time, he experienced much hardship and tribulation, and he never wavered in his revolutionary aspirations. Because of this perseverance, he was able to struggle and sacrifice in difficult circumstances, dedicating himself completely and achieving great achievements in revolutionary history. (2) Loyalty: Mr. Liao was a loyal follower of the Premier. Throughout his life, he shared joys and sorrows with the Premier, absolutely obeyed the Premier's orders and the party's discipline, knew only to shoulder obligations, and did not haggle over rights. He dedicated all his intelligence and talent to the party. This revolutionary red heart of loyalty should be emulated by comrades and compatriots today. (3) Diligence and integrity: Mr. Liao worked more than eleven or twelve hours a day, and sometimes even sixteen or seventeen hours. His hard work for national affairs is evident. Mr. Liao lived frugally. Although he held financial positions repeatedly, he remained upright and clean, with no surplus wealth in his family. This kind of integrity should shame corrupt officials. (4) Scholarship: Mr. Liao worked hard to learn in his youth. Even in his adulthood, while engaging in revolution, he did not forget to seek knowledge, constantly learning throughout his life. Therefore, his revolutionary will and spirit were always tense and vigorous, and his knowledge also increased with the times. This spirit of not forgetting to study while engaging in revolution is most worthy of emulation by revolutionaries. Today, as we welcome and bury Mr. Liao, on this day of serious national crisis with internal troubles and foreign invasions, we should emulate Mr. Liao's personality to promote the completion of our party's revolutionary cause and accomplish Mr. Liao's unfinished legacy. 1. Liao Zhongkai is not dead. 2. Liao Zhongkai was the Premier's loyal follower. 3. Liao Zhongkai was the savior of peasant and worker compatriots. 4. Liao Zhongkai's great personality is a model for comrades and compatriots across the country. 5. Emulate Liao Zhongkai's revolutionary spirit. 6. Welcoming and burying Mr. Liao means eliminating the Red Bandits and relieving the suffering of peasants and workers. 7. Welcoming and burying Mr. Liao means uniting sincerely to save the country from its crisis. 8. Welcoming and burying Mr. Liao means developing production and enriching national strength. 9. Long live the Three Principles of the People. 10. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang. 11. Long live the Republic of China. Shanghai Special Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang."

President Wang and Others Arrived in Shanghai

President of the Executive Yuan Wang Zhaoming, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Tang Youren, and Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming took the night express train from Beijing yesterday and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

Inspectors Chen Chunpu and Zheng Lin of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Nanyang Consulates Returned Home Yesterday; Impressions of the Consulates, Overseas Chinese, and Commerce

In order to inspect the consulates in Nanyang and to understand the actual conditions of commerce and overseas Chinese affairs in various places, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs specially dispatched Ministry Advisor Mr. Liang Zigaoxian, Standing Committee Member of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee and Director of the Overseas Chinese Education Department Mr. Chen Chunpu, and former Counselor of the Ministry of Railways Mr. Zheng Tao in February of this year. Mr. Liang departed slightly later due to other important business and is currently still en route. Mr. Chen and Mr. Zheng departed in early March and traveled through Annam, the Malay Peninsula, Siam, the Dutch East Indies, and the Philippines for more than three months. Recently, their mission completed, they returned home from the Philippines on the Empress of Canada, arriving in port at 1:30 PM yesterday. Director Yu Ming of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Wu Gonghu of the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau went to the port to welcome them. Accompanying Mr. Chen and Mr. Zheng were secretaries Su Hongbin and Luo Haiguang. Mr. Chen and Mr. Zheng issued a written statement of their impressions of their trip to Nanyang as follows:

The Mission's Tasks

According to them, the mission's tasks can be roughly divided into three categories: (1) inspecting consulates, (2) investigating commerce, and (3) investigating overseas Chinese affairs. More than ten people departed from Shanghai on the "Asama Maru No. 2" on March 9 and successively passed through Saigon, Singapore, Kuala Lumpur, Ipoh, Penang, Siam, Bangkok, Medan, Batavia, Bandung, Cheribon, Tegal, Semarang, Magelang, Yogyakarta, Surakarta, Surabaya, Malang, Zhangge, Garapalu, Wainanmeng, Bali, Makassar, and Manila.

Consulate Administration

Most consulates in various places are still diligently handling affairs, but it seems necessary to improve the institutional aspects. Consuls are originally commercial officers, and their responsibility is to promote commerce and protect overseas Chinese. In recent years, consulates in various places have conducted various investigations and statistics on local commerce, but there are still few efforts to obtain information suitable for actual needs to promote trade between them. Therefore, it is believed that the organization and administrative efficiency of the consulates cannot be improved without comprehensive planning. This matter is of great importance and cannot be accomplished without detailed regulations in the institutional aspects and improvements in personnel and finance.

Commerce in Various Places

As for the commercial situation in various places, Annam is said to be declining, with empty shops everywhere. On the one hand, this is affected by the economic downturn, and on the other hand, it is because the Sino-French Vietnam Trade Agreement has not yet been established, which affects trade between the two sides. If the Sino-French Vietnam Trade Agreement is concluded, China will establish consulates in Saigon, Haiphong, and Hanoi to promote commerce and protect overseas Chinese. The situation may improve in the future. The Malay Peninsula has a more reviving atmosphere. Recently, rubber and tin have seen slight improvements, so the commercial situation is better than in other places. In the Dutch East Indies, import and export are difficult due to heavy taxation, and the high exchange rate also hits foreign trade. In addition, the local people's knowledge is gradually opening up, and the position of our intermediary merchants is gradually being shaken. Overseas Chinese merchants in the Philippines are mostly retailers and timber merchants, and their operations are still acceptable. However, because the Philippines has been striving for independence in recent years, there is an organization of the National Economic Maintenance Association, which has some impact on the business of our overseas Chinese merchants. There have been repeated discoveries of the squeezing out of our overseas Chinese merchants recently.

Conditions of Overseas Chinese Compatriots

As for the overseas Chinese in various places, they are very concerned about the motherland, eagerly inquiring about the political construction in the country, etc., in great detail. Their sincerity in promoting domestic goods is no less than that of people in the country. Due to the influence of the dumping of goods from other countries, it is difficult for domestic goods to gain a foothold. However, if there can be a considerable organization in transportation, distribution, and economics, then the future can still be optimistic. As for the chambers of commerce in various places, those with relatively complete organizations, such as the chambers of commerce in Singapore, Siam, Medan, and Batavia, can indeed seek many benefits for the overseas Chinese. In terms of party affairs, there are many restrictions in British territories due to the exchange of documents, so there is little obvious achievement in the promotion of party affairs. Although the party headquarters in the Dutch East Indies can be open, work and activities are also difficult, so overseas comrades feel tired and exhausted this year.

Overseas Chinese Education

In terms of overseas Chinese education, in addition to visiting schools, we also held talks with the local education community to inquire about the local education situation and opinions. Here is a brief description of the situation in various places. In Annam, education is not yet developed, and the curriculum and teaching in various schools still need to be improved. Most schools still teach in local dialects and should switch to Mandarin as soon as possible. The management of overseas Chinese education in the Malay Peninsula is not bad, but a small number of schools teach English from kindergarten in order to receive subsidies from the local government. This point is not in line with national basic education. Overseas Chinese education in Siam is difficult to manage because the local government implements compulsory education, making it difficult for our overseas Chinese schools to operate. Overseas Chinese education in the Dutch East Indies is experiencing financial difficulties due to the economic downturn, but those who run the schools are still able to find various ways to support the past, which is commendable. Currently, the issue of registering with the local government has aroused the suppression of the Dutch East Indies government, which we regret. The purpose of our overseas Chinese schools is purely to cultivate young people and has no political effect. In accordance with the common practice of various countries, applying to the local government for registration is purely for the convenience of students returning to China to check their academic qualifications and has no other intention. The local government does not need to worry too much. Currently, this case is being negotiated, and we firmly believe that if the Dutch East Indies government can understand this point, it should withdraw its order. Overseas Chinese education in the Philippines is more free, but the results are less satisfactory. Overseas Chinese schools in the Philippines teach Chinese in the morning and English in the afternoon. In the hot weather, children have to attend classes all day and also read two languages, which is too tiring. They are also probably not capable enough. At the same time, the curriculum seems to be repetitive. For example, in the subject of arithmetic, there is a distinction between Chinese and English. This point should be studied. We feel that overseas Chinese in various places are very dedicated to running schools. If improvements can be made in the curriculum, teaching, and equipment, it will not be difficult to achieve perfection.

Returning to Beijing Within Days

In short, consulates are agencies for protecting overseas Chinese and promoting commerce, and their position is very important. In terms of administration, efforts should be made to improve efficiency and raise their position to facilitate the leadership of the overseas Chinese community. On the part of the overseas Chinese themselves, they should quickly seek unity, concentrate their efforts, and break the habit of each acting for themselves in the past, so that they may be able to save the current crisis by one in ten thousand. There are many other impressions, but due to time constraints, I cannot report them one by one, etc. After arriving in Shanghai, they are staying at the New Asia Hotel and the Oriental Hotel and plan to return to Beijing within the next day or two to report their inspection and return their mandate to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

The State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Took Over the Inland Waterway Routes Yesterday Morning; The Routes Were Taken Over in Three Ways; All Routes Operate as Usual

According to the Central News Agency, the lease period for the inland waterway routes of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has expired. The routes were taken over in three ways yesterday morning, and all routes operate as usual. It has been decided that the Zhenqing, Shenhu, and other five routes will be operated independently, and the remaining routes will continue to be tendered for commercial operation. The details are as follows:

Counting Account Books and Assets

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's takeover of the inland waterway route vessels was presided over by Chen Weiqing, director of the General Affairs Department and newly appointed manager of the Inland Waterway Steamship Bureau, dispatched by the head office. Mr. Chen, accompanied by takeover committee members Cai Pengcheng and Sheng Qunian, and bureau staff Zhang Yao, Li Rui, You Zhijun, and Zhu Zhilin, went to the bureau at about 9:00 AM yesterday to count account books and assets. In the afternoon, Mr. Chen went again to inspect and accept the various vessels, which were handed over by Zhu Yanping of the Department of Construction, lessee Zhang Jingpei, and Sun Yezhen, a staff member of the Inland Waterway Bureau.

Three Routes Depart to Take Over

In terms of outlying areas, they departed in three routes. For the Zhenjiang to Qingjiangpu route, the handover officer was Zhu Yanping of the Department of Construction, the Inland Waterway Bureau's Shen Songxian, and the takeover officer was Zhou Houkun of the head office. For the route from Zhejiang's Jiaxing, Xiashi, Hangzhou, Huzhou, Shuanglin, to Nanxun, the handover officer was Shen Zelin of the Department of Construction, the Inland Waterway Bureau's Yang Tingmei, and the takeover officer was Zhu Tianbing of the head office. For the route from Changshu, Suzhou, Wuxi, to Changzhou, the handover officer was Zhong Lisheng of the Department of Construction, the Inland Waterway Bureau's Zhang Jianfei, and the takeover officer was Feng Yuming of the head office. All three groups departed in turn.

Decision to Operate Five Routes Independently

After the bureau took over, it decided that the name would be the China Merchants Inland Waterway Steamship Bureau. The internal organization and personnel will not be changed for the time being. The bureau decided to operate the Zhenqing, Shenhu Ling, Shenhang, Shensu, and Suhang routes independently. The remaining routes will be tendered for commercial operation. If no merchant leases them, the bureau will operate them independently. However, none of the routes will be suspended. Yesterday morning, each route posted a notice from the head office, stating that they would operate as usual, it was said.

Chairman Chen Shuren of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee Talks About Government Relief for Overseas Chinese

Chairman Chen Shuren of the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee came to Shanghai on the afternoon of the 15th at 2:30 PM by early train from Beijing under government orders to discuss with Mayor Wu Tiecheng and others the welcoming of Martyr Liao Zhongkai's coffin to Beijing. A reporter from the China East News Agency specially went to his residence at Room 454 of the New Asia Hotel yesterday morning to visit him. He spoke in detail about the government's relief for overseas Chinese, etc.

The Status of Overseas Chinese

Mr. Chen first told the China East News Agency reporter that in recent years, due to the increasing economic downturn in various countries around the world, our overseas Chinese compatriots have inevitably faced some difficulties. The authorities of various countries, for the sake of their own people's livelihoods, inevitably have some conflicts with overseas Chinese in some jobs, resulting in acts of expulsion. However, our overseas Chinese compatriots, no matter where they live, have a certain characteristic, namely (1) diligence and frugality, (2) gentleness and respect, and (3) peaceful nature and hardworking. Moreover, because of their diligence, their production capacity is more specialized than that of the people of various countries, and at the same time, their wages are lower than those of the people of those places. Therefore, their position has gradually become consolidated in recent years. Although there have been anti-Chinese actions due to various reasons, most of them have been due to emotional impulses. After all, there are many places where various countries need overseas Chinese to help build, so they are very welcoming of overseas Chinese after the event.

The Mexico Incident as Proof

Mr. Chen immediately cited the anti-Chinese incident in Mexico two years ago as proof. At that time, the Mexican government was attacked by Labor Party members, which led to a fierce anti-Chinese movement. However, afterwards, the country needed overseas Chinese to help build, and the voice of Labor Party members opposing Chinese disappeared, because the country's national production and consumption are far inferior to that of overseas Chinese. Although there are anti-Chinese actions in various places now, after protests from various parties and government negotiations, a solution can definitely be found in the shortest possible time.

Relief for Overseas Chinese Compatriots

The government's relief for overseas Chinese is progressing simultaneously in diplomatic and internal affairs. If there are anti-Chinese incidents in various countries, the government is willing to serve as a backing for the people, arguing on the basis of reason. On the one hand, it is also working hard on its own construction. For example, the construction of Qiaole Village in Xuancheng, Anhui, opened yesterday. Government agencies have sent representatives to participate, which is sufficient to prove the government's emphasis on overseas Chinese compatriots. This move is to prepare in case overseas Chinese have to return to the country out of desperation. The government will naturally accommodate them and find a place for them to settle down, so that overseas Chinese compatriots can advance and retreat. At this time of serious national crisis, the government is planning relief measures for millions of overseas Chinese compatriots, it was said. Mr. Chen will be delayed in Shanghai for two or three days to welcome Mr. Liao's coffin, and will return to Beijing on the 18th.

Relief for Industry and Commerce Loans; Three Meetings Today; The Committee Guarantees Loans; Banks and Money Shops Directly Lend

According to the New News Agency, the Relief for Industry and Commerce Guarantee Loan Committee was established a few days ago, and Cai Zengji was publicly elected as chairman, with Du Yuesheng and Wu Xingya as vice chairmen. Chen Guangfu, Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoting, and Song Ziliang were elected as standing committee members. After a meeting was held on the 15th, the draft charter was discussed in detail and submitted to the chairman for correction. It was decided to convene the third meeting at 2:00 PM today to submit it for approval, and then report it to the Ministry of Finance to receive national treasury vouchers for safekeeping, officially start work,

Nature of the Committee

The nature of this committee is entirely to guarantee loans and does not directly lend. Any factory manufacturing domestic goods, store selling domestic goods, and exporter transporting domestic goods who requests a loan must submit a detailed form with information on assets and liabilities, profit and loss, purpose of the loan, and collateral to the committee for review. If the committee approves it after review, the committee will notify the banks and money shops to directly lend.

Lending by Two Industries

This relief for industry and commerce loans will be directly lent by various banks and money shops and will not be handled by a separate organization. Any factory or store requesting a loan will have its collateral reviewed by the Guarantee Loan Committee. The banks and money shops will then directly lend based on the notice from the Guarantee Committee, using the collateral of the factory or store as the first guarantee and the national treasury vouchers as the second guarantee, with a monthly interest rate of eight per thousand. The repayment period will be determined by both parties, it was said.

Martyr Yu Hongzhang's Tomb Commemorative Monument Unveiled Yesterday

Media representative Mao Chunpu reported on the circumstances of his martyrdom. The Shanghai Coal Industry Association, for their colleague Martyr Yu Hongzhang, who died for the country while participating in the rescue work during the January 28th Shanghai Incident, publicly buried him in the International Cemetery and erected a monument to commemorate him. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, representatives from various circles were invited to hold a monument unveiling ceremony at the tomb site. Attendees included Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce representative Yuan Hongjun, Red Cross representative Wei Tiezheng, Xianju Fellow Townsmen Association representative Wang Jingdong, Coal Industry Association representatives Mao Chunpu, Xu Yirong, Luo Dechuan, as well as family members and guests, totaling over two hundred people. The weather suddenly changed, and amidst the bleak wind and bitter rain, the mourning was further intensified. Immediately afterward, a meeting was held as scheduled, with Coal Industry Association representatives Mao Chunpu, Xu Wanrong, and Luo Dechuan serving as the presidium. After reporting on the circumstances of the martyr's death, representatives from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and the Red Cross successively delivered speeches. Finally, his elder brother Hongkui delivered a speech of thanks. Subsequently, he led the guests to view the tombstone. The event concluded at 4:00 PM. The inscription on the tombstone reads as follows: Yu Shanqing, courtesy name Hongzhang, was from Yin County, Zhejiang. He was born at the Yin hour on the 27th day of the tenth month of the third year of Xuantong. He died at the Shen hour on the 29th day of the second month of the 21st year of the Republic. His father, Mr. Yingchu, was in the coal business and established Dun Dacheng Coal Company on Zhili Road in Shanghai for several decades. He had seven sons, and Hongzhang was the fifth. He was born intelligent and resolute. In his youth, he was filled with patriotic thoughts. After the September 18th Shenyang Incident in the 20th year of the Republic, he immediately wanted to join the army, but his family prevented him. When the January 28th Songhu War broke out in the 21st year of the Republic, he organized a Red Cross rescue team with colleagues in the coal industry. Later, he joined the First Special Team and went to the front lines every day to carry out rescue work for soldiers and civilians. On the 29th day of the second month, during the fierce battle at Baziqiao, our army's position was lost and regained three times, with the dead lying on top of each other. Hongzhang, together with six members of the Eleventh Detachment, went to the front line on the morning of the 29th to rescue the wounded soldiers. When the vehicle reached the end of Baoxing Road, they proceeded on foot. At 10:30 AM, near Xingjiaqiao, they were spotted by enemy soldiers and shot, injuring his chest and thighs. He fell to the ground, bleeding. His companions carried him onto the vehicle and drove him and the wounded soldiers to Baolong Hospital. The rescue was ineffective, and he died at 4:00 PM in the afternoon. He was buried in the International Cemetery. He was 22 years old and unmarried. According to the rules of the International Cemetery, during wartime, rescuers from the Red Cross are not regarded as enemy combatants. Now, Japanese soldiers shot non-combatants, and their inhuman behavior is extreme. The world will have its own fair judgment on this. Our association is deeply saddened by Mr. Hongzhang's enthusiasm for loving the country and sacrificing himself for the country's difficulties. Therefore, we specially record the general situation and inscribe it on stone to inform the survivors and future generations.

Ministry of Railways Orders All Railway Bureaus to Revise Silkworm Cocoon Freight Rates, Effective July 21st

The Ministry of Railways yesterday issued an order to all railway bureaus to cancel the item "cocoons" listed in the previously promulgated list of special light and bulky goods, and to add two new items: "fresh or dried silkworm cocoons and wild silkworm cocoons," both of which are calculated as special light and bulky goods, effective from July 21st of this year. In addition, the item "field peas," originally listed as fourth-class freight, is now changed to fifth-class freight, effective from July 1st of this year.

Promotion of Commercial Acceptance Drafts: Chamber of Commerce Lecture Series Closed Yesterday Morning

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce held a lecture series to promote commercial acceptance drafts. Yesterday was the last session. Luo Qinghua, Deputy Manager of the Silk Industry Bank, delivered a closing speech and invited three experts, Zhu Xinong, Cai Chengxin, and Wang Xiaowen, to give lectures. Li Peilin took shorthand notes. More than 300 representatives from various industries listened to the lectures, and committee members Zheng Chengqing and Ma Shaocha provided hospitality. The speeches of each person are recorded as follows:

Luo's Closing Speech

Chairman Luo Qinghua delivered a closing speech, saying, "Today is the last session of the commercial acceptance draft lecture series held by our chamber. We are pleased to have economists Mr. Zhu Xinong and Mr. Cai Chengxin, and legal expert Mr. Wang Xiaowen, to grace us with their lectures. Representatives from various industries actively participated, which is extremely gratifying. In the past two sessions, experts were invited to attend and express their grand theories. The theoretical value of commercial acceptance drafts and the procedures for implementation have been elaborated in detail, which can serve as a reference for the actual promotion of various industries. The Silk Industry Association has been pioneering the use of commercial acceptance drafts for three months now. Although the subsequent promotion by various industries has not yet been popularized, the objective need for commercial acceptance drafts has become increasingly urgent with the excessive tightening of industrial and commercial credit. Since the financial turmoil last winter, there has been no hope of recovery for industry and commerce. Recently, the situation has become even worse, and the crisis is becoming increasingly pressing. The sharpening and concretization of panic phenomena cannot be overcome by superficial calmness. The stagnation of factory products is now worse than before, and the closure of factories and shops is also increasing day by day. The increase in the number of unemployed people is enough to worry about social security. As for the industrial, commercial, and financial aspects, the various credit instruments that various industries relied on in the past have now lost their function. The market chips have gradually become exhausted due to lack, and the credit of various industries has also gradually disappeared due to tightening. If the industrial and commercial sectors do not quickly create new credit instruments to replace them, then the difficulties faced by various industries will inevitably be ten or a hundred times greater than today. However, the creation of credit instruments has its objective conditions and cannot be expanded arbitrarily. The only other way for industry and commerce to create and use freely is the commercial acceptance draft. This is not only recognized by most experts but also the inevitable trend of various industries. Now, the silk and other industries have been implementing it for many days, and both buyers and sellers have benefited from it. It is hoped that other industries, after the elaboration and clarification by various experts this time, can quickly promote it, and Qinghua firmly believes that it will be able to achieve the goal of increasing chips and self-reliance. The holding of this lecture series will also be worthwhile."

Zhu's Lecture on Common Sense

Zhu Xinong lectured on commercial acceptance drafts and economic common sense: (1) What is a draft? (2) What is an acceptance draft? (3) What is the purpose of promoting commercial acceptance drafts? (A) Increase market chips; (B) Improve the account system; (4) What are the advantages of commercial acceptance drafts? A. Advantages for sellers: (A) In terms of capital operation: 1. The money will not be stagnant; 2. Capital turnover will be flexible; (B) In terms of cost reduction: 1. The discount rate is lower than any loan, then the seller can reduce costs; 2. There is no amortization of bad debts and loss of interest on outstanding debts, then the seller can reduce costs even more; 3. Reduce the employment of collection personnel, and costs can also be reduced. B. Advantages for buyers: 1. Using commercial acceptance drafts can reduce the cost of the seller, that is, directly reduce their purchase price; 2. There is no need to trade with cash, just use the sale price to pay the bills; 3. After the buyer pays the money on time and the credit is obvious, he can pay a capital and do several times the business; 4. The buyer must accept the bills on time, so he will not purchase goods at will. C. Advantages for the financial industry: 1. Commercial acceptance drafts are highly reliable; 2. The period is not long; 3. Can be re-discounted. D. Advantages for the entire financial market: 1. Adjust the surplus and deficit of finance; 1. Reduce the fluctuation of interest rates; (5) Conclusion.

Wang's Lecture on Law

Wang Xiaowen lectured on the ten legal viewpoints on commercial acceptance drafts: (1) The definition and types of acceptance drafts. The draft issued by the drawer is presented to the drawee by the payee, and the one signed and accepted by the drawee is called an acceptance draft. However, there are drafts accepted by banks and drafts accepted by merchants. The former is called a bank acceptance draft, and the latter is called a commercial acceptance draft. However, no matter what its type, its legal nature is the same. (Refer to Article 49 of the Bills of Exchange Law) (2) The legal view of commercial acceptance drafts. The so-called legal view of commercial acceptance drafts refers to the nature and effect of commercial acceptance drafts in the Bills of Exchange Law. Now, according to the provisions of the Bills of Exchange Law, the characteristics and effects of commercial acceptance drafts are explained separately as follows: A. Commercial acceptance drafts are fully indicative securities. (1) What is a security? Any right on paper is related to the paper itself, that is, the right on paper arises from the creation of the paper, and this kind of paper is a security. (2) What is an indicative security? Indicative securities refer to securities that instruct others to pay money and other things to a third party. In principle, they can be transferred by endorsement (refer to Articles 710 and 716 of the Civil Code), and the exceptions are prohibition of transfer or transfer by delivery (Article 27 and Article 21, Paragraph 4 of the Bills of Exchange Law). (3) What is a complete security? Those who cannot claim rights without the security are complete securities. (Refer to Article 15 and Article 16 of the Bills of Exchange Law) B. Commercial acceptance drafts are not securities of cause. The debtor of a commercial acceptance draft absolutely bears the obligation of a certain amount due to the bill behavior (refer to Article 2 of the Bills of Exchange Law). No matter what the reason is, even if the issuance of the draft is based on illegal behavior, if a third party obtains the draft, there is no deception or malice, or no gross negligence, the debtor shall still be responsible (refer to Article 10 and Article 11 of the Bills of Exchange Law), which is different from civil bills that need to inquire about the cause.) C. Commercial acceptance drafts are formal securities. The issuance of drafts must meet the legal requirements (refer to Article 21 of the Bills of Exchange Law), otherwise, it will be invalid according to law (refer to Article 8 of the Bills of Exchange Law). Therefore, whether the three-linked checks and bank notes issued by our country's money houses are the bills of exchange referred to in the Bills of Exchange Law is worth studying. That is, the commercial acceptance draft format drafted by the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank also has problems in law. D. Commercial acceptance drafts are formal securities, that is, the liability of the debtor is based on the words recorded on the bill (refer to Article 2 of the Bills of Exchange Law). The meaning of its words cannot be changed or supplemented by other evidentiary methods. (3) In addition, there are many legal points related to commercial acceptance drafts, but it is impossible to complete them in a short time today. Now, they are specially listed for amateur research. If you have any questions, you can send them directly to the design department of Taiping Insurance Company, No. 212 Jiangxi Road, and they will be answered in detail. A. Issues of forgery and alteration of bills (Article 13 of the Bills of Exchange Law) B. Issues of signature or record deletion of bills (Article 14 of the Bills of Exchange Law) C. Issues of bill of exchange time limit (Article 19 of the Bills of Exchange Law D. Endorsement issues (Articles 27 to 38 of the Bills of Exchange Law) E. Acceptance presentation issues (Articles 39, 41, 42, and 45 of the Bills of Exchange Law) F. Participation acceptance issues (Articles 55 to 61 of the Bills of Exchange Law) G. Guarantee issues (Articles 50 to 54 of the Bills of Exchange Law) H. Payment and participation in payment issues (Articles 66 to 81 of the Bills of Exchange Law) I. Recourse issues (Articles 81 to 102 of the Bills of Exchange Law) J. Protest issues (Articles 103 to 110 of the Bills of Exchange Law)

Cai's Speech

Cai Chengxin said, "Mr. Luo Qinghua asked me to talk about the situation abroad in the third lecture on acceptance drafts. Recently, because I have been busy with work, I have not had time to make systematic preparations, so let's just talk about it haphazardly. The history of drafts is very long. About 300 years ago, merchants in Venice and Florence, Italy, had already used drafts due to practical needs. The Bills of Exchange Law formulated in the United Kingdom in 1882 has a very clear explanation of commercial acceptance drafts. As for places such as the United States and Canada, the development of acceptance drafts is relatively backward. This method was only available about 110 years ago, but it was not very important. Since the world economic panic in 1929, the market chips have suddenly tightened. Therefore, commercial acceptance drafts are strongly advocated. In terms of numbers, according to approximate estimates, the acceptance of chestnuts for the whole year last year was probably worth 700 to 800 million yuan. In Canada, it is about 100,000 to 200 million yuan. Because the statistical methods in the United Kingdom are incomplete, accurate figures are more difficult to obtain. The above is a general overview of the popularity of acceptance drafts overseas. Our country's current economic situation also needs to promote this method. Therefore, this time, Mr. Luo Xiaohua and others actively advocated it, which is definitely not a blind attempt, but an acceptance of the valuable experience of others. Because under the current situation, the market chips are so lacking, the banking industry cannot but shrink very much for accounts receivable. However, we are unwilling and unwilling to stop the market like this for a long time. Therefore, we can only think of remedial methods to make the silver root looser and the market more lively, in order to overcome this recession. Now we find that commercial acceptance drafts are the most conducive to meeting the current needs, so everyone has the obligation to do their best to promote them. As for the various advantages of acceptance drafts and the methods of implementation, the previous gentlemen have already explained them in detail, and I will not repeat them here."

The City Received a Timely Rain Yesterday: The Weather Turned Cooler and People's Hearts Tended to Peace: The Hardworking Farmers Were Overjoyed

Since the beginning of summer, the city has been suffering from a long drought for a month. Most people are worried about the return of drought. However, the weather changed drastically yesterday afternoon, and it rained heavily until it stopped at night. The fields and rice paddies recovered slightly, and the farmers were overjoyed. The rice price also shrank after the rain. The details are recorded as follows:

Timely Rain

Since the beginning of summer, there has been a long drought without rain, and the weather has been hot and dry, which is likely to cause a major drought. Yesterday morning, the weather was extremely hot, with the temperature reaching about 90 degrees Fahrenheit. In addition, the sky was hazy with clouds, making it feel even more sultry. At 12:45 PM, it suddenly drizzled, drifting with the wind. Then, the raindrops gradually increased, and soon water dripped from the eaves until it stopped slightly at 5:45 PM. However, the vaulted clouds were still densely covered, and it still looked like it was going to rain again. Yesterday, the rainfall from noon to night was about three to four inches. As a result, the heat gradually subsided, as if it were cool autumn weather.

Fields and Rice Paddies Recovered Slightly

Since the drought, the cotton fields and rice fields in various districts of the city have shown signs of dryness between the fields. Farmers irrigate day and night, fearing the return of drought. Everyone is worried. After the heavy rain yesterday, although the rainfall failed to realize the ideal desire, this adjustment will be a small supplement to the long-drought fields. Regardless of cotton, rice, and other grains, relying on this natural irrigation, they have recovered slightly. Therefore, the farmers turned their worries into joy. According to the old farmers, yesterday's weather was cloudy, and it is predicted that not only Zhejiang and Shanghai will have rain, but also other provinces in Jiangnan.

Rice Price After Rain

The price of rice in Shanghai has been rising continuously since last week due to the dry weather and the difficulty of transportation, which has reduced the source. The No. 1 (i.e., special) rice in the North City has exceeded the price limit set by the municipal government. Other Chen Xian foreign rice and other rice have also risen by more than half a yuan. Yesterday was a weekly holiday, and the market only traded in the morning. By the time the market closed at 12:00 noon, the rice price was still the same as the previous day. However, according to the Soybean and Rice Industry Association Committee Qiang Guisheng, the market situation was stable this morning (i.e., yesterday) and there were no ups and downs. When the heavy rain suddenly fell in the afternoon, the weather turned cooler, and the drought was slightly reduced. People's hearts gradually stabilized. Therefore, it is predicted that the rice price will shrink back when the market opens tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning). If there is more rain to adjust, the autumn harvest will not be damaged.

This council hopes that residents in the concession who own dogs will have their dogs vaccinated to prevent rabies. Let this be known to all." Signed by acting Director-General Pediot.

Short-Clothed Bandits Apprehended on Race Course Road; Fake Gun Too Realistic; Four Bandits Detained for Investigation

The head of the Chengdu Road Patrol Station, believing that theft cases have been frequently heard of late, with robberies on Race Course Road being the most common, ordered detectives to patrol strictly within their jurisdiction. Yesterday at 1:25 PM, detectives Huang Fusen and Bao Shi Guichun from the patrol station saw four men in short clothes walking towards them on Race Course Road. Finding their behavior suspicious, they joined with Chinese Constable No. 1725, Shang Xue, to question them. When the men hesitated and stammered, they were stopped and searched. A fake gun, difficult to distinguish from a real one, was found on one of the bandits. All four were taken to the patrol station. It was learned that the four bandits were named Wang Afu (who had the fake gun), Zhang Zaiqing, Gao Zhenghe, and Zhang Di Yi. The patrol station's lawyer, Qian Jiu, stated the facts of the case to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Special Court, saying that due to time constraints, the patrol station had not yet investigated the four defendants, so he requested permission to detain them. Judge Liu Yugui questioned Wang Afu and the others briefly and ordered them to be detained pending further investigation.

Wang Yin Nian Impersonates Official; Swindles and Deceives Everywhere; Many Official Documents and Letters of Appointment Confiscated; Victims Summoned to Testify

Wang Jinian, a Ningbo native who previously worked in Nanjing political circles and is now 27 years old, has recently been unemployed, staying in Shanghai at Room 36 of the Xinhua Hotel in Hongyunfang, Huage Street, French Concession. To resolve his issues of food and clothing, he had the wild idea to impersonate the chief of the Jiangsu Salt Affairs District dispatched by the Salt Administration Reform Association of the Executive Yuan, swindling and deceiving money everywhere and issuing letters of appointment. Chen Guangfu, a fellow townsman living on Jisi Feier Road, sought to become the secretary-general. Wang demanded 1,500 yuan for expenses, of which 100 yuan had already been paid. Lin Zhijun and Fei Baolin were each defrauded of $15, and Zhou Peikun was defrauded of $10 in an attempt to secure a minor position. The scheme was discovered by Jin Jiulin, inspector of the French Patrol Station, who dispatched detectives Xu Jinlong, Yin Baoke, and others to Room 36 of the Xinhua Hotel on the previous day, arresting Wang. Confiscated were 181 official document covers of the Salt Administration Reform Association of the Executive Yuan, a bundle of blank letters of appointment, 1,000 envelopes of the Fourth District of Jiangsu Salt Affairs, 500 blank official documents, 19 letters of appointment with various titles filled out in the name of Wang Jinian, district chief, a square seal with the seal script "Salt Administration Reform Association of the Executive Yuan," and three small seals with the names Wang Jinian, Wang Jichun, and Qian Junkui, as well as a glass frame inscribed "Congratulations to Mr. Yinian on his glorious appointment," signed "Lin Bing Respectfully Congratulates." All were taken to the patrol station, and Wang was detained. Chen Guangfu and others who had been defrauded were summoned to the station. The next day, they were sent to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, where Judge Wang Gangxu conducted the preliminary hearing. Lawyer Yuan Jiahan explained the facts of the case and requested a two-week extension for a detailed investigation before filing the indictment. Detective Xu Jinlong reported on the arrest of the defendant and the seizure of evidence, and presented the various forged documents seized. Chen Guangfu and others complained about being defrauded and paying money. Wang Jinian confessed to the charges of impersonation and fraud. The court ordered a postponement until the 26th for further investigation and interrogation. The defendant was returned to custody.

Prostitute Buys Diamond Ring; Pays with a Bounced Check; Jewelry Store Files Lawsuit; Reconciliation at the Trial

Prostitute Yi Jun, the third oldest, hung up her sign to solicit business at her brothel located at No. 7, Fuzhili, Pingwang Street, Fuzhou Road, last month. In February of this year, she selected a diamond ring worth $200 from Wanyuan Chang Jewelry Store at No. 41, Old Jiaochang, Xinbeimen, and paid with a check. However, when the check was presented for payment, the funds were unavailable. After repeated demands for payment, Liu Qianzeng, the manager of Wanyuan Chang Jewelry Store, filed a lawsuit with the Criminal Division of the First Special Court, accusing Yi Jun of fraud. The lawsuit stated that on February 23 of this year, Yi Jun selected a diamond ring from Wanyuan Chang Jewelry Store, stating that the price was $200. The defendant claimed that she did not have enough cash with her and promised to deliver it the next day. The plaintiff, being familiar with her, did not suspect anything and handed over the ring. However, she never returned. When they repeatedly went to her brothel, Yijun, to demand payment, she always made excuses and claimed that the ring had been pawned, even showing a pawn ticket. The plaintiff originally intended to report her to the authorities, but the defendant repeatedly begged for leniency and promised to find a way to pay. On April 24, she issued a check for $100 from the Ningbo Industrial Bank, but when it was presented for payment, the bank stated that the check had no funds associated with it and was essentially a bounced check, a very deceptive act. Her actions constitute the crime of fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Code and should be arrested and punished according to the law. The plaintiff also requested the court to order the defendant to pay $200 in damages. The court approved the filing and scheduled a hearing for the previous day. However, Yi Jun, knowing that she was in the wrong, urgently asked someone to mediate with Liu Qianzeng and quickly returned the money. Liu had already accepted the payment, so when the case opened the previous afternoon, Liu declared that the case had been settled and requested withdrawal. The court ruled that the case would not be heard.

Two City Councils Held Meeting Yesterday; Relieving Stores on Rongshi Road; Letter to French Municipal Council Urging Swift Relief

The shops in the Caishi Road area of the French Concession, due to the French Municipal Council constructing roads on that road and piling up soil on the sidewalks in front of the shops to a height of half a zhang, have been unable to leave or even walk into the shops, and during normal times, the ashes and sand fly about. When it rains, there is standing water in front of the door, making it slippery, resulting in the absence of customers. As the market is in extreme depression, the shops are barely able to maintain themselves. With the impact of the current road construction, they all feel that they are sitting around waiting to die. They especially signed their names and sealed the petition to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association and the Fourth and Fifth District Branches of the Shanghai Municipal 1st District Citizens' Association, requesting assistance. The Fourth and Fifth District Branches of the Municipal Association held a joint meeting of committee members at the Anxin Temple, Baire Road, at 4 PM yesterday. The committee members in attendance were Cen Zhiliang, He Yaozhang, Tong Wenli, Ye Ruiqi, Xia Shanxiao Tong Lizhang, Sun Ruiting, Zhang Zhimin, Huang Zhixian, and Xu Yanwu from the Fourth District; and Zhang Qingfa, Fang Bocen, Qian Yuan, Xi Jingyan, Qu Zhenhua, Wu Yunshou, Xu Zixian, Yan Chengxian, Hu Zifang, Zhang Huichang, and Gu Gongda from the Fifth District. Ye Ruizhai was elected chairman. The chairman reported on the letters from the various shops, and after a long discussion, the following resolutions were made: (1) The two associations will jointly write a letter to the French Municipal Council, urging them to provide swift relief. (2) The letter will be forwarded to the General Association to quickly seek relief measures. (3) A rent reduction committee will be organized to first distribute rent survey forms and the names of the landlords, and then write to persuade them to voluntarily reduce rents in order to maintain operations. (4) According to the association's investigation report, the construction workers demanded one or two yuan in drinking money from the shops when piling up soil, under the pretext of leaving a passage. The association should report this situation to the French authorities for attention and prompt prevention. Before appropriate relief measures are sought, the workers should be ordered to move the soil to a suitable location in order to facilitate business operations. The above resolutions were announced, and the meeting adjourned.

There are also many photos of famous scenic spots in Ningbo and Zhenhai.

Five Countries Send Personnel to China to Investigate Our Country's Currency; Financial Circles in This City Express Welcome

The Central News Agency reports that the governments of the five countries of Britain, America, France, Italy, and Japan have reached an agreement and will each send financial representatives to China to investigate the monetary situation of our country. The British representative has been appointed as Sir Otto Niemeyer, a financial advisor, and the French representative has been appointed as Mr. Renouvin, the financial deputy counselor of the French embassy in Britain. They are expected to begin their journey to China in August. The American, Italian, and Japanese representatives are expected to be announced soon. The financial circles in this city welcome the joint arrival of the financial representatives from various countries to China to investigate the currency. It is also transmitted that when the representatives of various countries come to China to study the currency issue, they will divide the currency into two types, one for domestic use and one for foreign use. The currency for domestic use will still be based on silver, and a new method will be agreed upon for the currency for foreign use. The opinions of the financial circles in various countries on this new method are all based on the technical position of each country. Britain advocates that China's foreign currency should be linked to the pound, France advocates that it should be linked to gold, and the United States advocates that it should be linked to the dollar. Our country's financial circles believe that this matter is very inappropriate. It is hoped that the representatives of various countries will come to China and base their work on our country's national conditions and current situation, and not solely on the technical position of each country.

Jiangsu Province Work Relief Summary of各省旱災義振會 (Each Province's Drought Relief Association)

According to Cheng Junsheng, director of the Jiangsu Province investigation and distribution, the 各省旱災義振會 (Each Province's Drought Relief Association) recently reported that Zhu Qicheng and others, work relief director of Jintan County, have reported that he has traveled to the hardest-hit areas in the 5th and 6th districts together with the county magistrate to conduct on-site evaluations of the reservoir locations. He said that the former Qing Dynasty soil administrator, Ke Zhuang, when he was the prefect of Zhenjiang, built many reservoirs that benefited the people of Tan Township. These were recorded in historical records. These reservoirs have all been in disrepair for many years and have been leveled. Now, it is proposed to rebuild these reservoirs to truly benefit the people. Regarding the regulations on the custody of work relief funds in Jiangsu, the staff of this office and the work relief directors of various counties are all unpaid volunteers. The necessary administrative expenses are issued by the association in accordance with regulations. After the work relief funds are received by the investigation and distribution director, they are distributed to the work relief directors of various counties in accordance with the plan, and then transferred to local public organizations for safekeeping. The local public organizations of each county organize a work relief fund custody committee to be responsible for safekeeping and to accept the entrustment of the work relief director. According to the payment vouchers issued by the director, they are issued to the foremen for distribution to the workers. The investigation and distribution director is responsible for the overall work relief in the province, properly planning and supervising the implementation. The work relief directors of various counties are responsible for completely and fundamentally helpful work relief, and the pre-construction work plans must be approved by this office before implementation.

Work Relief Regulations Measurement, mapping, and calculation of earthwork shall be assisted by county government personnel. This office's work relief shall select mountainous areas lacking water, and areas most severely affected by disaster in the county, and recruit disaster workers to open reservoirs for water storage. The number of reservoirs opened shall be determined by the amount of work relief funds in the county. The length, width, depth, and amount of work for each reservoir shall be estimated before construction begins and reported to the association for verification. The price for opening a reservoir in this office is set at 15 cents per cubic meter. The recruitment of disaster workers shall be handled by the district chiefs under the direction of the county government. Each reservoir shall have a foreman who is responsible.

Chongming Shanghai Association Opposes, Shengshan Sijiao Returning to Zhejiang, Yesterday's Membership Meeting Resolved to Telegraph the Government for Ardent Efforts

The islands of Shengshan and Sijiao, etc., originally under the jurisdiction of Chongming County, Jiangsu Province, recently have been requested by groups such as the Ningbo Tongxian Association to be placed under the jurisdiction of Dinghai County, Zhejiang Province, by the government. The Chongming Shanghai Association specifically held a membership meeting yesterday, attended by over a hundred people including Tong Xingbai, Yang Zhen, Wang Lemin, Chen Yinchu, Shi Fujiu, Tong Muge, Chen Dongbai, Song An, Xu Peixing, Chen Xiangxin, Zheng Xiong, etc. Yang Zhenzhong presided, with Chen Dongbai as the recorder. It was unanimously decided to telegraph the government for ardent efforts. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Respectfully to Chiang, Chairman of the Wuchang Headquarters; Huang, Minister of the Interior in Nanjing; Chen, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government: We have recently read in the Shanghai newspapers of June 15th that the Ningbo Fellow Association, etc., convened a general meeting on the 2nd of this month and unanimously decided to submit a request to Your Excellencies to transfer the islands of Shengshan, Sijiao, etc., under the jurisdiction of Chongming County, Jiangsu Province, to the jurisdiction of Dinghai County, Zhejiang Province. After reading this, we are extremely perplexed. The islands of Sheng and Si have always been under the jurisdiction of Chongming and have a long history. Moreover, the water of the Yangtze River is clear, and the water of the Qiantang River is turbid, with a clear distinction between the two. This is a natural boundary in terms of topography between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The position of the remaining Si islands is clearly in the Yangtze River, so in terms of topography, it clearly belongs to the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces convened representatives to Beijing for public discussion by the Ministry of the Interior regarding the issue of boundary demarcation. Based on historical and geographical relations, it was resolved to continue to use Huanglong as the focus of the boundary between the two provinces. The case has been finalized and there are no objections. However, not long after, the Ningbo Fellow Association, etc., suddenly wanted to overturn the settlement and change the jurisdiction. This matter concerns the change of provincial boundaries and the overturning of the original plan of the Ministry of the Interior. We respectfully request Your Excellencies to take into consideration the historical geography and other various relations, and to deal with it seriously in order to avoid disputes. This would be greatly appreciated. In this urgent telegram, we await your orders. Chongming Shanghai Association kowtows.

Cotton Spinning and Weaving Experimental Museum Officially Bids for Construction

The Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Committee and the National Central Research Institute, in view of the fact that the technology of the mechanical textile industry in our country is backward and the production methods are not known to be improved, which greatly affects the development of agriculture and industry, have jointly formed the Cotton Spinning and Weaving Experimental Museum to actually study its advantages and disadvantages in order to seek improvement. The initial operating cost is 400,000 yuan, of which the Cotton Control Committee will undertake 250,000 yuan, and the Central Research Institute will undertake 150,000 yuan. The museum site has been surveyed and determined to be in the southeast corner of the Central Research Institute on Billy Nan Road, covering an area of 15 mu, with a value of approximately 70,000 yuan. The housing part has been planned by architect Dong Dayou as a completely new type of factory building. The cost is set at 90,000 yuan, and bidding was officially opened yesterday. After the decision is made, construction can begin. All the complete set of machines are purchased from countries such as Britain and Germany, with a value of approximately 200,000 yuan. Instruments and books are approximately 40,000 yuan. The annual recurring expenses are entirely borne by the Central Research Institute. Its organizational system is the same as that of the Central Research Institute, that is, researchers, assistant researchers, clerks, etc., are established under the director. The candidate for the director has been decided to be concurrently held by Zhou Zijin, the director of the Engineering Experiment Institute of the Central Research Institute. Currently, one professional technician and four researchers have been hired. In the future, the scope of work of the museum will focus on the improvement of the textile industry, the improvement of quality, and the improvement of technology, and will replace domestic textile and dyeing factories in studying their shortcomings and conducting various practical experiments. In the spring of this year, the Cotton Control Committee specially sent Li Zhuangshoujun to Japan to study the situation of the Japanese textile industry so that they could learn from it in the future.

Municipal Farmers Association Requests the Ministry of Industry to Reward Domestic Pyrethrum, Dependence on Foreign Lands in the Past Was a Huge Loss, Promoting Planting to Benefit Farmers' Income

The Municipal Farmers Association yesterday submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to reward the domestic "Samsung Chrysanthemum" insecticide invented by the China Chemical Industry Society in order to promote it. The original text said, "In order to request the award of domestic pyrethrum 'Samsung Chrysanthemum' to demonstrate promotion and save losses, please review this matter. Since the Austrian discovery of pyrethrum in 1506, which has the function of killing insects, countries have competed to plant it. Japan and the United States export more than 10 million yuan worth of it every year. Our country also relies on foreign countries, and the losses are huge. In view of this, the China Chemical Industry Society of this city has created farms since the sixth year of the Republic of China, engaged in trial planting. Over the past eighteen years, after several improvements, the farm area has increased to more than 300 mu, focusing on selecting seeds, cultivating seedlings, and signing contracts with farmers to cooperate and promote planting, sparing no effort. It also held grand ceremonies in the early summer of the twenty-second and twenty-fourth years to entertain people from all walks of life to visit. Mayor Wu of this city personally attended the meeting and awarded the name 'Samsung Chrysanthemum' to show promotion. I think that the company, as a private enterprise, in order to seek the popularity of new crops, does not hesitate to make huge sacrifices. Its spirit and ambition are really commendable. It is definitely not the same as those who only care about quick success and instant benefits. The total annual consumption in the farm is no less than several thousand yuan. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt, if the planting of 'Samsung Chrysanthemum' can be promoted and popularized, it seems to be a small supplement to the income of farmers. It is hoped that this will help to prevent losses. Thinking about this, I would like to ask the Ministry to issue an order to commend and promote it, so that the people of the whole country will naturally follow the government's promotion and widely plant it. This will not only prevent losses but also be a policy to save the rural economy in the midst of rural collapse. Is it appropriate? I respectfully ask you to review and follow it. Respectfully presented to Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, Shanghai Municipal Farmers Association respectfully presents."

Tidbits

— (Baling)

When he has no lover to attack him, Wei is very complimentary to him. Once he is attacked, and therefore withdrawn or resigned. Then, those who follow to attack him are the ones who compliment him at the time. This situation, I have tested, is 90% true. But now it is really getting more and more difficult to be a person.

People will say bad things about others, and never admit their own faults. Therefore, the world is full of good people, or it can be said that the world is full of bad people.

People only feel the preciousness of being employed when they are unemployed. The same place is too much.

The life of a contributor is slightly off. Is very painful. When a manuscript is completed, it is like a pregnant woman waiting to give birth. When you see your work. Revealed in the newspapers. That's like a pregnant woman giving birth smoothly. Just as happy.

Blacksmith

— Huang Kewei

Ding dong... Ding ding dong...

Bare-chested, the strong arms bulged with hard chestnut flesh. Gripping the heavy iron hammer, hitting the red iron again and again, sparks flew like golden stars, the brilliance of life!

They are blacksmiths, young, brave, standing up to do it all day long, exchanging their sweat for white rice! Although blood and sweat soak their bodies, and flames scorch their skin, they have no sighs, no sorrows!

They grow up in a world of iron and fire, in the breath of coal and smoke. Their whole bodies are dark, their eyes are full of red tendons, and their hairy bare legs are wrapped in burlap bags to resist the invasion of sparks. Near them, a pair of great iron-melting furnaces is burning, grinning and opening its blood-red mouth. Greedily and tirelessly devouring large chunks of coal, the long nose spewing hot air, filling the entire low house.

From morning to dusk, night to dawn, they keep on, keep on beating iron; ding ding dong, ding ding dong, forever echoing that simple, loud tune!

Concubines and Oxen

— Zhang Huang

In common sense, the first wife is the domestic helper, and the concubine is the man's sexual instrument, the rich man's toy, entertainment item, decoration, and they themselves are parasites. Enjoyers! It is well known that there are many falsehoods, and there is so-called ironclad evidence!

In my hometown, there is a countryman named Zhu, who originally worked as a rent runner (that is, he was sincerely hired by the landlord to collect rent on his behalf in the countryside); several families in the town who owned fields in Xixiang entrusted him to collect them along the way. He obtained the due remuneration from the employer, and was able to report less and more to collect the reimbursement of food and accommodation expenses from each owner, and he could also get a little commission when the owner had land sales and purchases. Over the years, he gradually accumulated a well-off family from a poor man.

After the annual harvest season, he set off to run rent in the Xixiang area. This is the identity, authority, and self-respect of the landlord's representative, which makes the tenants awe him. When he encounters food and lodging, he naturally instructs the tenants to provide them without having to spend money. Later, for several years in a row, he selected palace girls from the farmers and brought five or six strong young girls back to his home as his concubines.

Zhu had a thin foundation of fields and acres in his hometown. When he brought so many concubines home, he assigned them to agricultural work one by one, ploughing the mud, transplanting rice, carting water, weeding, harvesting. The workers cooperated and were able to command as they wished, greatly increasing the output. He often exaggerated his brilliant calculations in front of people: "I keep these women, just like a few plowing oxen, but I don't need to spend money to buy oxen. They can do the same work as plowing oxen, and they are more intelligent than plowing oxen and are willing to listen. Even if you compare them to hired workers in the fields, you can save a lot of wages, and everyone will protect the family wholeheartedly. As for the fun of the boudoir, the heat is just as good!"

Unfortunately, Zhu, who was the most scheming, gradually contracted atrophy and can no longer get out of bed. Seeing that the crowd of women are crowding each other, and the sounds of chickens crowing and dogs barking can be heard every day, they let the field work be abandoned, which has been in short supply for a long time, and there is no way to clean it up! As a result, he made himself a plow ox's plow ox, and finally could not handle it!
