Free Talk

Affirmation and Negation in Literature

— Zhang Xiangshan

A realist writer, due to contradictions in their worldview, can create the greatest tragedy through the interplay and conflict of affirmation and negation in their works.

The affirmation and negation referred to here are the same as those in philosophy.

Needless to say, a writer who is faithful to reality will depict it without mercy. Such a writer's work will inevitably present both the negative and affirmative aspects of reality. For example, in the works of Balzac and Gogol, the nobility and feudal landlords are presented as the negative, and the middle class as the affirmative.

A writer ahead of their time affirms this affirmative aspect, inevitably leading society forward onto a path of development, essentially acting as a guide for this new society.

Although Gogol's works aptly depict both the affirmative and negative aspects, Gogol himself said that his works were "laughter through tears." Indeed, the laughter in his works is tinged with tears. Why? Because he was saddened by the incompetence of certain people. If, in his works, affirmation could defeat negation (i.e., understand the inevitable decline of certain people and strive for affirmation), then there would be no tragedy! However, he reinforced affirmation by more stubbornly emphasizing negation, pitting them against each other, thus creating tragedy! Because the reality emphatically declared the development of affirmation! Laughter emerged from tears. For the above reasons, Gogol was merely an outstanding writer of truth, merely a critical realist. His hope for the revival of negation prevented him from becoming a writer ahead of his time, because, as mentioned above, he did not guide the new society.

Therefore, the most appropriate method for addressing negation and affirmation in works is to portray negation as a process of affirmative development, depicting the gradual demise of the negative aspect, thereby further highlighting the vibrant growth of the affirmative.

Some critics believe that in such a chaotic modern society—especially in the society we live in—emphasis should be placed on the depiction of negation, because the incompetence, dead ends, and evils of the negative aspect need writers to truthfully express. Moreover, because contemporary writers mostly come from the intellectual class, they are distant from active existence in society, making it difficult to understand that active existence. Therefore, the description of passive existence becomes necessary, and this task is within the reach of modern writers. Describing passive existence means emphasizing the depiction of negation.

We find this argument somewhat mechanical, because it severs negation and affirmation, limiting itself to the depiction of negation. Its achievement is only exposure or critical realism, which is not what we need.

At this point, perhaps readers will raise a counter-question, "Then should we focus solely on affirmation!" In fact, focusing solely on affirmation is also a mistake. Although we know what the future society will be like, it is by no means an abstract thing. It is what historical practice tells us. We can imagine, but we cannot deviate from practice. If we only describe affirmation and abandon negation, then such affirmation becomes a world conjured up by a magician, not something transformed from the negative aspect.

Recently, I finished reading a very good work, Sholokhov's "Virgin Soil Upturned." This work not only depicts the process of collective farm development, but also provides us with excellent lessons on the handling of affirmation and negation.

Sholokhov takes Davidov, the leader of the collective farm movement, as the affirmative element, artistically and accurately placing him on the front line. At the same time, the White Army Captain Polovtsev and the wealthy Yakov Lukich, as the negative elements, without a hint of objectivism, work in opposition to Davidov in a truthful manner, realistically depicting the demise of the negative and the advancement of the affirmative. It is precisely through this fundamental conflict of forces that diverse and positive characters emerge, creating new scenes. Through individual postures, social pathos is born, enabling readers to better understand the difficulties and growth of a developing society.

Therefore, in depicting truth, we need to address affirmation and negation mutually, without emphasizing one side. Relying on a progressive worldview, we should portray the demise of the negative as an expression of the growth of the affirmative.

Dusk

— Mo Fu

…Suddenly, a decision arose in his heart; and all the knots were completely untied. His chest felt as empty as a vast wilderness. His wife's withered face, the miserable cries of his four children… suddenly fled from his memory, no longer troubling him.

He walked along the bustling street, as if walking in a desert, completely unaware of the vehicles, horses, and pedestrians surrounding him, all rushing about for survival. What flashed before his eyes could not attract his attention, nor could his ears hear the noisy din. He followed behind the person walking in front of him, like flowing water, as if there was an unknowable, invisible line connecting them.

Half an hour later, he stepped into a true wilderness. He didn't know when it started, but he was all alone, swaying his body westward! The sun, hiding behind the deep blue, black mountains, emitted spoke-like rays of light, forming semi-circular gear teeth. Surrounding him were scarlet, red, and purple clouds, moving about. From behind him, a layer of thin darkness surged in the distance; this was the opposite of dawn, growing thicker and thicker, constantly changing.

The sun withdrew its last brilliance from this sinful world, and everything in the human world seemed to disappear with it.

He moved his legs indifferently, controlled by some external force, his hands clasped in front of his chest, his eyes empty, facing the boundless grayness.

He crossed the fields, walked to the riverbank, and stopped. There was no wind. The pale yellow moon rose above his head, reflected on the smooth, mirror-like surface of the water. He stared at the moon's reflection in the river, motionless, like a sorcerer praying for the departed. Continuing for about three minutes, he suddenly plunged into the river as if seized by thought—this sudden action surprised him greatly, but in that instant, he felt truly liberated—delivering a tragic blow to the drowsy and sensitive dusk, the trembling sound floating straight into the sky. The smooth water surface, at this time, seemed like molten glass boiling in a furnace, many white mounds rising high on the river surface, tumbling and dancing. The pale yellow moon's reflection, agitated by the water, rippled and disappeared.

The night deepened, and silence returned.

Porter

— Wan Shisi

Outside the borders of people's dreams,

We gather at the pier,

Like the dead faces of comrades!

The gray sky: high, and vast!

In the barge: the siren wails.

Heavy sacks tightly clasp our spines.

We, hastily, carry them from the warehouse to the ship,

And from the barge…rush to the shore!

Ceaselessly panting, ceaselessly

Pulling soiled sleeves, wiping away sweat!

We are so uncomplainingly bowed down,

Grunting—grunting, bearing the weight on the ground!

Many legs, stepping in unison,

We are steadfast and strong…

Every day we awaken the metropolis,

From our eyes: the morning sun rises!

Insect Trap Lamp

— Xu Ying

During the busy farming season, our school regularly had a "busy leave," allowing adults to cut wheat and plant rice, allowing women to cook meals, deliver food, and bail water, and allowing young children to tend cattle, carry babies, and watch the threshing ground. In the evening, if the weather was too hot and it happened to be a bright moonlit and starry night, people who had worked hard were willing to take advantage of the cool breeze, and we would invite them to gather at the Guandi Temple! In the square in front of our school gate, everyone brought their teapots and pipes, and casually chatted.

At the beginning of this chat session, we made a special effort to hang up a gas lamp from the New Year's temple fair. Its dazzling light immediately dimmed the bright moon, and we also hoped that everyone could take this opportunity to review their thousand-character primers, recite the "Elementary Reader," or tell stories while being able to see each other's smiling faces. But things turned out unexpectedly. Insects from all directions followed the neighbors from all directions and came to the gathering. We saw locusts flying all over the yard, mole crickets crawling everywhere, and older children fought and tore at each other in competition, causing a chorus of crying. Millions upon millions of leafhoppers and moths covered the lamp, and scarab beetles rose and fell like flying stones, hitting people's heads. Mosquitoes and gnats were like dust in a hurricane, everywhere. In this way, order was greatly disrupted. Not only did we not feel the refreshing night breeze, but everyone was covered in sweat.

Seeing this situation was like opening an old account book. I suddenly remembered that when I was a pest control worker, I had caused a great disaster because of an oil lamp. This incident made me feel guilty every time I thought about it. Originally, we were allowed to speak freely at the chat session, so I tried to extinguish the fire in the lamp. With everyone's eyes suddenly in darkness, I clapped my hands heavily to stop the noisy shouts.

"Today, I have a story to tell you all, please pay attention.

A year or two ago, I was doing pest control work in a place. All the insects that came here today were the ones I had to catch. I caught them and killed them to prevent them from harming the crops. At that time, our method was not only for us to catch them, but also to ask everyone who farmed to catch them together. We knocked on every household, explained the reasons, and asked them to help.

"We wanted every household to install an electric light in their own field, with a large basin of water under the light, of course, the water couldn't soak the light. We also wanted them to sprinkle a little kerosene in the basin. As you have read in books, insects are afraid of the smell of kerosene, and kerosene on insects kills them. Sprinkling kerosene in the cesspool eliminates maggots..."

After the lamp was extinguished, the crowd was silent for a moment, but soon there was noise again. Children cried, laughed, and shouted sharply. Adults whispered, and the sound of pipes knocking on the ground rang out… Women dropped things, borrowed matches, and struck matches, the firelight stirring the vision of those in front and behind. It was difficult for them to grasp my words completely. Even when our cooperative distributed loans and we spoke, it was like the bursting of bubbles in an oil pan.

"I asked them to prepare. We provided the equipment, and they provided the oil. Can you guess if they followed the method we told them?…"

I had to speak with even greater force and make the words ripple to get the audience's minds moving a little. However, the effect was still not great.

"They are not as smart as you all. They didn't believe our words at all. On the night they lit the lamps, I rode my bicycle to check, and only four or five places had the lights on. The rest all lit the lamps in their own houses, the men slept, and the women mended clothes. You may not realize it, but these few families who lit the lamps suffered greatly…"

I waved my hand and said in a louder voice:

"Just like today, insects from all directions came to these fields. There were too many insects, and the insect trap lamps were useless. These fields, these good people, are still scolding us for causing them to have no harvest. Many people who didn't light insect trap lamps were also saying, 'Look, look, I knew it would be harmful.' Everyone, did we harm them, or did the farmers' lack of cooperation harm them?——For this reason, the school, not because it's afraid of spending money, but because it's afraid that this place will suffer this kind of harm again, in the future; this lamp will no longer be lit.……"

After that, we each bring incense sticks to our summer evening chats, never lighting a lamp again.

Little Girl's Sweetheart

Artificial Madman (Part 1)

— He Luo

One,

The father was a kiln owner with twenty or thirty kiln workers who, from the ninth watch to midnight, drilled underground, excavating the treasures of the earth for him. His property accumulated like piles of coal.

The mother was also a venomous shrew, specializing in hitting her daughters-in-law on the head and stomach, capable of causing them to miscarry. Their backs and legs were also covered in scars.

The madman was their fourth son.

By the time he was twenty, he had grown into a very sturdy young man. His arms were very strong, and like his parents, he grabbed the kiln workers by the hair, refusing to let go. But letting go was even worse. Bricks, stones, or wooden sticks—anything he could get his hands on, he would use to strike. If he picked up a kitchen knife, he would threaten to cut off people's ears.

Although his parents were a little worried that he would cause trouble, the ones he beat were ultimately kiln workers. According to their reasoning, kiln workers depended on kiln owners for a living. Without kiln owners, kiln workers wouldn't know how to live, except by begging.

Sometimes they would boast triumphantly, saying that kiln workers were born bad seeds, and if you didn't give them something spicy, they wouldn't know your kindness.

But unfortunately, something happened. The kiln workers, who conquered nature and created wealth by drilling underground, only cared about extracting coal. After they emptied the earth, it suddenly collapsed, crushing seventeen people to death. Seventeen people were crushed into a meat paste, indistinguishable from each other.

After that, the kiln owner's business deteriorated day by day. The newly hired kiln workers were lured away by other kiln owners after only a few days. In the end, only three or five people remained, supporting the declining facade.

The kiln owner's family also changed from covert infighting to open warfare. The methods previously used to deal with kiln workers were now used at home. Father and sons argued from morning to night, and from night to morning, and as they argued, they began to fight, resulting in bloodshed.

The most reckless of them was their fourth son.

He had learned all the techniques of cursing and hitting people since he was a child. Now he could knock down his mother with a headbutt. If his father picked up a stick, he would pull and push, tripping his father to the ground. Before his father could get up, he would loudly curse and shout, running out into the street.

It could be said that the brothers were like vicious dogs, very good at gnawing at heels. They constantly glared, raised their eyebrows, puffed out their chests, cursing as soon as they opened their mouths, and hitting as soon as they reached out. Seven or eight hands, like tendrils, wrapped around someone, and everyone rolled to the ground together, rolling and tumbling, making it impossible to see who was hitting whom.

University Days (4)

— Written by German Storm, translated by Chen Yinzhi

Renali was not among them: she stood alone not far from the door, gazing at the girls with a slightly melancholy air; they were talking lively, not showing any restraint in other people's gorgeous house: they simply didn't pay attention to her.

There is nothing more selfish and cruel than young people. But after I came in, the mayor's wife also came in. She greeted these young people, and after scanning the hall with her "general's gaze," as Fritz said, she walked up to Nali and took her hand. "In order to make dancing pairs able to match each other," she said to the dance teacher, "please line up the boys according to their height!"—The dance teacher did as she said, and at the same time, she also went to the girls, wanting to arrange them in the same way. The daughter with the golden hair of a sudden morning, was the tallest, almost a head taller than the others. She was placed on the wall opposite us: but then the difficulty came out. "I don't know, Charlotte," said the mayor's wife. "Who is above and who is below you and Nali, because in my opinion you are the same height!"

This Charlotte was the daughter of a court attendant and judge, and she stepped back. "Miss Nali is probably taller than me," she said softly.

"What's wrong, my lady," my friend's mother called to her, "come out of that corner of yours, and compare with Miss Nali!"

The little girl had to come out, back to back, to compete with the tailor's daughter. But—my eyes saw very clearly that she had the ability to make the craftsman's daughter's black head hardly touch her head.

This little girl was wearing a light-colored dress. Renali was wearing a black woolen dress with red stripes, with a white crepe shawl around her neck. The color of this dress was too dark, giving a strange feeling, but it was a perfect match for her.

The mayor's wife compared the two girls for a while. "Charlotte," she said, "you used to be the first beauty; but you have to be careful not to let her surpass you! I think she is going to surpass you."

Hearing this, I seemed to see the little girl's black eyes sparkle.

Shen Bao Pharmaceutical Weekly

Report on School Health Inspection in Qinghai

— Zhang Wenshan and Shao Xiaxian, Qinghai Provincial Health Laboratory

The Health Education Committee has been established since the end of last year, and it has been five months since then. Initially, due to the severe cold and long winter vacation, as well as the fact that medical personnel were all part-time, it was delayed until April 13th that the committee began to carry out its main task, "School Health." Although this started late, it was also due to environmental factors, which were unavoidable.

Due to the lack of medical personnel, the committee can only go to various schools in the afternoon to implement health education and treatment. Currently, ten schools have started. Once there are sufficient medical personnel, all primary and secondary schools in the provincial capital will be started, so as to enable young men and women to obtain good health education and habits, as well as the happiness of a healthy body, so as to become the elites who will promote health undertakings in the future. Now, the statistics of shortcomings after the health examination are classified as follows:

Total number of people examined: 482 (including 188 from the First Middle School of the Muslim Progress Association, 140 from the Second Primary School, all male; 154 from the Affiliated Primary School of the First Women's Normal School, including one male, the rest female)

Number of people with shortcomings: 406

Total number of shortcomings: 1002

Types of shortcomings:

Poor eyesight: Mild 55, Severe 12, Most Severe 3, Total 70

Ear diseases: 44

Trachoma: Mild 86, Severe 63, Most Severe 28, Total 177

Other eye diseases: 36

Dental diseases: Mild 89, Severe 45, Most Severe 2, Total 136

Tonsillar hypertrophy: Mild 121, Severe 75, Most Severe 17, Total 213

Lymph node enlargement: Mild 75, Severe 8, Most Severe 1, Total 84

Malnutrition: Mild 92, Severe 20, Most Severe 2, Total 114

Skin diseases: Mild 107, Severe 29, Most Severe 13, Total 149

Weak heart: 4

Weak lungs: 14

Orthopedic surgery: 7

Rhinitis: 95

Goiter: Mild 38, Severe 5, Most Severe 1, Total 44

Inguinal hernia: 1

Phimosis: 12

From the above table, it can be seen that young male and female students are not all healthy. Although they attend classes every day, the soundness of the individual cannot be discovered without a physical examination. The examination method used by the committee adopts the health examination format promulgated by the Central Health Administration as the standard, including weight, height, vision, hearing, nutrition, as well as ears, eyes, mouth, nose, heart, lungs, spleen, lymph nodes, thyroid gland, reproductive organs, etc. All are included in the examination. The results obtained are indicated by symbols such as "mild," "severe," and "most severe" to indicate the severity of the shortcomings and whether urgent treatment or correction is needed. These are the key points after the health examination. However, due to the lack of hospitals, systemic examinations such as urine and blood cannot be obtained, and important shortcomings cannot be corrected. This is also a regrettable matter for the committee. For example, tonsillar hypertrophy and the resection of phimosis cannot be treated without surgery and hospitalization. It is hoped that people in society will enthusiastically create hospitals for the promotion of health undertakings, so as to benefit the general young men and women and build a future for society and the country.

Wrongful Imprisonment Compensation and Medical Lawsuits

— Song Guobin

The National Lawyers Association has recently been working hard to promote the movement for compensation for wrongful imprisonment, and has designated June 5th as a publicity day. This movement to protect human rights is truly an unprecedented initiative in China's thousands of years of history, and its significance is extremely important. In a country ruled by law, the government has a legal responsibility to protect the people. Unfortunately, if a wrongful imprisonment occurs, the people suffer losses in reputation, body, spirit, and property, and the government bears the responsibility for failing to protect the people's legal rights. A civilized country cannot eliminate all lawsuits, but it also cannot allow wrongful imprisonments to exist. Compensation is merely a remedy after the fact! On the one hand, it allows the victims to partially compensate for their losses in reputation and money, even if only a tiny amount. On the other hand, it makes those who make false accusations more cautious and makes judicial officers act with care. The intention is very good, and the law is very beautiful. However, this good law, which prevails throughout Europe, has not yet been realized in our country under the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun. This is truly regrettable. Now, because of their profession, the lawyers have personally witnessed the many wrongful imprisonments. They are speaking out and working hard to remedy the situation. We believe in the good intentions of these benevolent people, and we should unite to support them and promote the early realization of this movement.

The number of lawsuits is increasing day by day, and it is not known how many of them involve wrongful accusations. How can this be seen? It can be seen in lawsuits between doctors and patients. As a member of the medical community, I have heard and seen many cases of patients suing doctors! But the result—the doctor wins in most cases—from this, it can be seen that most of the patients' accusations against doctors are false accusations. In the world, there is only one truth. If this is right, then that is wrong; if this is wrong, then that is right. Therefore, there can be no situation where the plaintiff and defendant are both right or both wrong. If the defendant loses the case, then the plaintiff's accusation is legitimate. If the defendant wins the case, then the plaintiff's false accusation is undeniable. If false accusations do not carry the responsibility of compensation, then not only are human rights not protected, but the nation's most solemn law is also treated like a cheap trifle. If the cause of the loss is due to a judge's misjudgment, then the responsibility for the wrongful imprisonment should be borne by the judicial officer, which is a matter of utmost fairness. Furthermore, I have heard that reputation is a person's second life, and for the medical profession, a good reputation is especially the standard. Once a patient makes an accusation, the newspapers report it, and society condemns it, and the reputation is already widespread. Regardless of the outcome of the case, the reputation, which is difficult to obtain but easy to lose, has already plummeted. Therefore, in medical lawsuits, the loss of reputation suffered by doctors is huge, while money, spirit, and body are secondary. Even if the falsely accusing patient is later compensated by the court, the former reputation cannot be restored in a short time, let alone if there is no compensation at all. Some people think that the patient's accusation against the doctor is not completely intentional false accusation, but mostly due to their lack of legal knowledge, which is understandable. But the study of medicine is very specialized, and it is common for diseases to be incurable. Whether the patient died from the disease or from the doctor is difficult for even medical experts to observe objectively, let alone for patients who know nothing about medicine. Therefore, in terms of legal knowledge, patients are merely insufficient, but in terms of medical knowledge, patients have none at all. To speak recklessly without knowledge is either out of temporary anger or out of intentional extortion. If compensation is not required, how can the number of medical lawsuits be reduced in the future? Therefore, I hereby express this to the medical community, to the patients who sue, and to the arbitrary judges.

Common Sense Q&A About Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(59) Acute Articular Rheumatism

(Question) What is acute articular rheumatism?

(Answer) It is a disease in which multiple joints acutely become painful and swollen, and the whole body is feverish.

(Question) How does this disease occur?

(Answer) This disease is also an infectious disease, but the pathogen is unknown. It is probably an infection of streptococcus or staphylococcus, which occurs as a heterotypic or epidemic state.

(Question) What are the triggers for this disease?

(Answer) Colds are often triggers for acute rheumatism; secondly, unsuitable housing and bad weather can also trigger this disease. It is especially prone to occur in the season of moldy rain and humidity.

(Question) Is there a relationship between this disease and occupation and age?

(Answer) Those who engage in rough labor, such as rickshaw pullers and maids, are most likely to suffer from this disease. The age group of 15 to 35 years old is the most common.

(Question) When acute articular rheumatism is about to occur, what are the initial signs?

(Answer) The patient feels tired all over the body, easily fatigued, and the limbs are stiff. There are also various mucosal inflammation symptoms.

(Question) After the disease has already occurred, what symptoms appear?

(Answer) The joints are affected very rapidly, especially the large joints of the lower limbs; then multiple joints are affected. In most cases, the disease spreads from one joint to another immediately.

(Question) Does the patient's body have a fever like other infectious diseases?

(Answer) Yes. But the fever is not very high. It rarely exceeds 39 degrees Celsius. The rise in temperature follows the course of the joint disease. Whenever a new joint is affected, the body temperature will rise once.

(Question) Are there systemic symptoms at the same time as the fever?

(Answer) Yes, sometimes. Like headaches, dizziness, and hot flashes, etc.

(Question) What are the local diseases that occur in the joints in acute articular rheumatism?

(Answer) It mainly affects the synovial membrane of the joint, the joint capsule, or the tendon sheath, and the mucous bursa; occasionally it affects the muscle membrane and muscle sheath. Initially, inflammation occurs in the large joints, especially the knee, foot, elbow, or hand joints, then it spreads to the shoulder and hip joints, and finally it affects the small joints such as the wrist, ankle, and fingers. The affected joints generally show redness, swelling, heat sensation, and pain, which are the typical symptoms of inflammation. The pain is very severe, so the movement of each joint is hindered.

(Question) Do changes occur in the circulatory system at this time?

(Answer) Acute articular rheumatism often affects the heart; therefore, it is often associated with endocarditis, pericarditis, and myocarditis.

(Question) What about endocarditis?

(Answer) In endocarditis during rheumatism, the mitral valve or aortic valve is most often affected. Warts form on the inner surface of the valve. As a result, mitral valve insufficiency or stenosis, and aortic valve insufficiency occur.

Common Sense of Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene

— Tang Renjin

(51) Chronic Suppurative Otitis Media (commonly known as otorrhea)

Speaking of a symptom of chronic suppurative otitis media, it is generally known as otorrhea. It mostly comes from the transfer of acute otitis media. As seen in clinical diagnosis, this disease accounts for the largest number of various diseases in otology. It is especially common in childhood. This is because the causes of acute otitis media (such as measles, scarlet fever, whooping cough, smallpox, pneumonia, etc.) are also most common in childhood. Among them, especially in

Page 16

When suffering from acute otitis media, without proper treatment, or due to malnutrition, or due to adenoid weakness, it is easier to transfer and become chronic suppurative otitis media.

The most obvious suffering felt by patients with chronic suppurative otitis media is hearing loss and tinnitus. Sometimes pain, headache, head heaviness, dizziness, nausea, vomiting, and staggering gait can occur. If we use an otoscope to examine, we can see that the external auditory canal often has erosion. Pus exists in the depths. The nature of the pus is different. Sometimes it is muco-purulent. Sometimes it is purely purulent. The pus sometimes emits a specific foul odor. Its amount varies, and there is no certainty. If this purulent secretion is wiped clean, the perforation of the eardrum can be observed. The location, shape, and size of the perforation are different. However, the eardrum perforation of this disease is mostly a large perforation. It will never be as small as that of acute otitis media. When the disease is severe, the eardrum can be completely missing. There is usually only one perforation. The shapes are mostly round, oval, heart-shaped or kidney-shaped. The location is usually only two types: central and marginal. When the entire eardrum is missing, or in the case of a large perforation, the mucosa of the tympanic cavity is often seen. It is rose-red, or yellowish-red, or purplish-red. It is often swollen. The surface is either smooth or uneven. Granular granulation occurs. Sometimes it forms a pedunculated aural polyp. Therefore, it hinders the discharge of pus, and causes many dangerous complications. In addition, there are so-called middle ear cholesteatomas. It can often break down bone. This is also a sign that is very easy to cause dangerous complications. As for the most dangerous period of this disease, it is when obvious bone ulcers and osteomyelitis form. Secondary meningitis, brain abscess, sinus thrombosis, pyemia, or severe massive hemorrhage caused by the disease eroding the blood vessel wall, etc. Because they all have a bearing on life, I dare not say the prognosis of this disease is good, and I dare not say it is bad. However, in patients who are physically strong and well-nourished, if proper treatment can be performed early, dangerous results can be avoided and a cure can be obtained. However, the otorrhea patients I have seen in clinical practice have mostly had the disease for one or two years if less, and more than ten years if more. Some have even reached old age. At this time, the disease is unusually complicated. If you want to completely cure it, it is not easy. At the same time, it is still necessary to prevent the arrival of dangerous complications. Therefore, this disease is best to implement appropriate treatment early. Do not delay the time. It is necessary not to treat it.

Popular Talk on Modern Venereology (5)

— Chen Shengbai (Compiled) Yin Muqiang (Proofread)

Chapter 7 On the Treatment of Syphilis

Mercury and iodides have long been effective drugs for syphilis. Recently, there have been arsenic and bismuth agents.

Looking at the history of syphilis treatment, our country is not inferior to Europe and the West. The administration of mercury preparations was already seen in the Zhou Dynasty. According to medical records of the Zhou Dynasty, light powder was often used to treat damp poison. The components of the medicine and the goal of treatment were in line with mercury preparations. Other treatments, such as Smilax glabra and Tenfuling for treating scabies, are also the same in nature as Sassafras, which was used to treat malignant minor poisons in Western history. Unfortunately, later generations did not study it and there was no progress.

Since the 20th century, effective drugs have emerged one after another. However, the above-mentioned several types still do not lose their inherent value. As for the adaptation of each drug, it is said that arsenic preparations should be used in the first stage (Sal-v-arsan 606 is its representative). Mercury preparations are used in the second stage (injectables have recently been changed to bismuth preparations because of their peaceful nature and few side effects). Iodide is used in the third stage. However, one must not be too rigid. The most appropriate method is mixed therapy. (That is, arsenic preparations are the main ones, supplemented by other preparations.) This is because when two different drugs act on the pathogen at the same time, their sterilization effect is more significant than using one alone.

The earlier syphilis-specific drugs are used, the more obvious the effect. As the disease progresses, the effect weakens. Therefore, a definite diagnosis must be made as early as possible when the initial hard chancre is discovered. Begin full treatment.

Furthermore, when administering drugs, we should also find ways to avoid drug resistance (Arzneifest). Drug resistance refers to the fact that when chemical drugs act on pathogens, the residual pathogens develop resistance to the chemical drug due to insufficient drug dosage, resulting in ineffectiveness when administered again. The existence of this chemical resistance can be transmitted to ten or hundreds of generations without end. Therefore, insufficient treatment of syphilis not only fails to alleviate its symptoms, but also increases the resistance of the pathogen to the drug, and makes those who are subsequently poisoned fall into an irreparable situation. Now, looking at the social situation, any prostitute or any person infected with poison is almost in a state of drug resistance. This is why the disease cannot be eradicated and the spread of poison is increasing day by day.

Witnessing this crisis, Hoftmann advocated the so-called extreme dose therapy. The American medical community even continued to use arsenic and bismuth preparations for injection for one year in an attempt to completely eradicate the poison. This can be called an unusual army in the syphilis treatment field. Recently, countries in the East and West have followed suit and achieved remarkable results. However, in our country, due to the decline of scientific knowledge and insufficient economic capacity, it is difficult to see its implementation. It still needs our supervision and hopes for self-reflection from patients.

Chapter 8 The Problem of Syphilis Prevention

Preventive medicine occupies an important page in the medical field of the 20th century. Syphilis is no exception. However, syphilis prevention is not like the use of preventive vaccines for cholera and typhoid fever, nor is it like the isolation of leprosy. It is also not comparable to cleaning food and drinks for cholera, typhoid fever, and dysentery. Since we know that the first medium for transmitting syphilis is sexual intercourse, then to achieve the purpose of prevention, ideally, banning sexual intercourse is the most appropriate. Unfortunately, this is not possible in reality. Therefore, the problem of syphilis prevention is more difficult than other infectious diseases. Now, let's discuss it in terms of general prevention and individual prevention.

(A) General Prevention Since the harm of syphilis affects society and the country, general prevention is essential.

Zi. Legal and Compulsory Prohibition A Prostitution Problem Since prostitutes are the location of syphilis nests, the disposal of prostitutes is an important part of prevention. Therefore, there is advocacy for

(1) Abolishing Prostitution Although abolishing prostitution is a simple method of preventing syphilis, if we do not find a way to resettle these abolished prostitutes, it will cause them to be displaced and easily change from public to secret. The proliferation of private prostitutes in countries that have abolished prostitution (such as the United States) is due to this.

(2) Public Prostitution System and Venereal Disease Examination Movement This is to implement regular inspections under police supervision. Those who are poisonous are prohibited from receiving customers. Those who are non-toxic are allowed to engage in the industry. However, superficial and incomplete inspections are ineffective. If strict inspections are carried out, it can be concluded that all prostitutes will be banned as poisonous. This will cause major social problems. Although, there are indeed flaws in the implementation of public prostitution and venereal disease examination. However, according to the percentage of knot calculations, it has indeed decreased significantly. It seems to still have its value. It is worth emulating.

The Medicine of Pain Relief (19)

— Li Xing

People ask, how exactly does one relieve pain? The method of pain relief that is in line with pathology should first be the hydrotherapy and heat therapy method of pain relief. This method can be said to be completely beneficial and harmless. This method is the hot compress method. It is better to use a saturated solution of cold and hot magnesium sulfate. Magnesium sulfate solution has the effect of eliminating movement and relieving pain, and is completely harmless to the body. In addition to magnesium sulfate, the heat of water is also very important. When heat is applied, the blood vessels in the boil area will dilate. When the blood vessels dilate, the tension in the affected area can be relaxed, and the pain is reduced accordingly. Apply a short-term cold compress immediately after applying heat, which can prolong vasodilation and prolong the effect. In addition to the relaxation effect, increasing the blood flow rate also increases the function of excreting toxins, and the benefits are not small. It is also quite good to apply analgesic ointment or lotion.

The first point to note is to avoid danger. We know that bacteria can easily enter the blood from boils. If it invades the blood, it will be difficult to save, so when the boil matures, the boil should be cut off or the feet should be cut off to allow pus and toxins to flow out of the incision to reduce the risk of invading the blood. As for furuncles, some people think that surgery is not possible. This kind of argument can be considered reasonable, but it can also be considered unreasonable. It is reasonable to say that it is useless to have surgery too late for furuncles. It is unreasonable to say that death after a knife for a long furuncle cannot be considered to be caused by the surgery, because the patient will die without surgery. According to the opinion of a famous surgeon, furuncles should be operated on earlier, because performing appropriate surgical operations can indeed reduce the mortality rate. If the surgical operation is too late and cannot save the patient, it can be avoided.

Cellulitis is a type of acute disseminated inflammation in tissues. The reason is that toxic bacteria invade the skin and flesh, causing suppuration, ulceration, or gangrene. Cellulitis often starts in the legs, hands, or face. The onset is often an inflammation that starts from a small break in the skin and spreads to the entire limb in a short period of time, which is similar to the saying, "A single spark can start a prairie fire." The bacterium that causes this disease is often streptococcus. On the one hand, this bacterium causes severe acute inflammation in the area, and on the other hand, it often invades and endangers the patient's life in a short period of time.

The principle of treating this serious problem is roughly the same as the principle of treating boils. Pain can be relieved as much as possible within the possible range, but do not misuse anesthetics and oral painkillers to reduce the patient's resistance. The urgent task of saving life is to cut open the rotten area greatly to allow toxins to flow out, and at the same time, the gauze applied to the wound should be soaked in concentrated liquid to absorb toxins. At this time, it is more hopeful to use surgical operations to save lives. Never hinder the operation to cut off a glimmer of hope.

An abscess is a local suppuration. An abscess is similar to a boil at the beginning, but it is larger than a boil. At first, the best way to reduce swelling and relieve pain is hydrotherapy with cold and hot compresses, the effects of which are detailed above. Secondly, lifting up the swollen area and resting can often prevent suppuration. If you want to avoid suppuration and surgery, faithfully implement the above principles. This will not only relieve pain but also prevent pain before it happens. If pus has already formed, the least painful way is to have surgery to release the pus. Once the pus is released, the pain can be reduced by eighty or ninety percent. Not having surgery will cause more pain, the pain will last longer, and there is also danger.

Hemorrhoid pain

The lower end of the large intestine and the anus are extremely prone to problems. When there is a problem, there will be pain every time you have a bowel movement. If the pain is not treated, it can last for ten or twenty years without healing. Ordinary people often say, "(Nine out of ten people have hemorrhoids,") although this statement is inevitably exaggerated, it can be seen that there are not a few people who suffer from hemorrhoids. Only true scientific medicine can relieve the patient's pain. The pathology, prevention methods, pain relief, and treatment methods of hemorrhoids are briefly described below for readers' reference. Hemorrhoids are divided into external hemorrhoids and internal hemorrhoids. The following is a brief description of each.

Among external hemorrhoids, the more common one is thrombosed external hemorrhoids, which are found outside the anus and range in size from soybeans to walnuts. The larger it is, the more painful it is. The reason for the development of this type of external hemorrhoid is often that coughing or forceful rupture of the venous tubes in the anus causes blood to flow under the skin to form a blood clot, which is thrombosed hemorrhoid. Sometimes inflammation of the veins at the lower end of the rectum can also cause thrombosed hemorrhoids. The characteristic of this type of hemorrhoid is that there is no hemorrhoid in normal times, but it is suddenly discovered. This type of external hemorrhoid is most painful at the beginning due to the tension of the blood clot. When the hemorrhoid is large, it is unbearable to walk, sit, or lie down.

The most effective and reasonable method for relieving this type of pain is to use a little local anesthetic to cut open the hemorrhoid and squeeze out the blood clot, so that the pain is completely eliminated in a short period of time. The wound will be completely healed in just a few days. If this method is not used and palliative treatment methods are used, such as applying analgesic ointment, having a bowel movement every day, and using hot and cold compresses, the blood clot can gradually disappear on its own. However, the pain must be prolonged for one or two weeks. Sometimes an abscess can also develop in the hemorrhoid, because bacteria are very easy to grow in old blood clots. If it becomes a sore, the pain will be prolonged. Note that external hemorrhoids cannot be treated with injections. This is the general treatment method for thrombosed external hemorrhoids, and patients can choose for themselves.

Regarding the clinical symptoms of this disease, there are not many that can be specifically mentioned; diarrhea is a very important symptom, but constipation may also occur sometimes. Abdominal depression and abdominal pain are mostly absent. In addition, there are anemia, weakness, emaciation, and other systemic conditions; increased temperature is also very common, but it is impossible to determine whether it occurs in the intestine or in the lungs. Sometimes, in the cecum part of the lower abdomen, a tumor can be found just by going through the touch examination procedure: this is also a type of intestinal tuberculosis, the so-called ileocecal tuberculosis. His passage is generally very slow; because of the atrophy and hardening of the intestine here, the intestinal orifice is also unusually narrow. This type of patient is mostly adolescents during the youth period, and recovery requires surgery. Proof of tubercle bacilli in the feces cannot be taken as evidence of this disease, as this can be caused by swallowed phlegm. The examination of the intestinal part of the light is of great help in the diagnosis of intestinal tuberculosis; the detailed situation in this area is, of course, not so clear to those other than experts.

The treatment of intestinal tuberculosis can be divided into two aspects: one is diet control therapy, and the other is drug therapy. Regarding food control, if the sufferer has constipation, all mild laxatives must be used with caution, and it is best to eat more fruits and fresh vegetables. If diarrhea symptoms occur, then foods such as cabbage, snap beans, fatty meats, and cold drinks should be prohibited, or at least reduced to a considerable extent. It is best to add a little lime water to the internal service of milk: coffee should also be prohibited. Keeping the abdomen warm is beneficial to abuse, so various therapies such as sun lamps are helpful. In drug therapy, astringents are the most important: agents such as blood powder, kaolin, tannic acid, and 　 are very suitable. Long-term injection of calcium agents is also very beneficial for diarrhea symptoms. The application of opium preparations has the effect of stopping diarrhea and relieving pain.

The State of Secondary Education in Our Country

— Xing An

The underdevelopment of education in our country is a clear and obvious fact. According to recent statistics from the Ministry of Education, the number of people receiving secondary education in our country is only twelve per ten thousand, ranking twenty-sixth when compared to major countries around the world. From this, one can imagine how far behind our country's education is.

In all civilized countries around the world, primary education is a form of compulsory education. All children within the country, upon reaching school age, have an obligation to receive primary education. Not only that, it is said that some countries have even implemented a compulsory system for secondary education. However, in our country, not to mention secondary education, even primary education, though nominally designated as compulsory, is actually received by very few school-age children nationwide.

But based on the facts, secondary education should also be listed as a form of compulsory education. This is because in today's complex social environment, a young person needs adequate abilities to cope, and a few years of primary education is simply not enough. However, given the current state of education in our country, hoping to enforce compulsory secondary education is impossible. But finding ways to gradually popularize secondary education should be an issue that cannot be ignored.

The underdevelopment of secondary education in our country has many causes. For example, the lack of educational funding, the shortage of educational talent, and the weak capacity of the people to afford secondary education are all factors. Another reason is the lack of widespread primary education. The solution, of course, should be to improve the situation from all aspects.

Random Notes, Part 1

— Xiao Ying

Recently, there seems to be a trend toward revivalism, and as a result, the images of the past have been stirred up in the minds of many.

Naturally, its value is evaluated differently depending on each person's perceptions. Is this evaluation genuine or false? This, it seems, has not yet been definitively determined. Perhaps it's because of the passion for revivalism? No, rather than the passion for revivalism, it's more appropriate to say it's the extension of divine authority. Underneath this, for some reason, people's faith in gods has become remarkably strong recently. Yes, "gods" can control people's minds, "gods" can bestow blessings or bring disaster, and "gods" can also satisfy the different desires that different people cherish in their hearts.

Every person, unless there is a deficiency in their constitution, naturally has a kind of aspiration. Some of these aspirations are limited to the present, while others transcend reality and reach intangible fantasies. Thus, burning incense and worshiping Buddha arise in response to the times. Saying this may be a bit flawed, because burning incense and worshiping Buddha have a long history and are not sudden occurrences in reality. However, based on the lack of spiritual sustenance, this form has become even more widespread.

Recently, I received news from someone from Xiaoshan that a ferry departing from Shaoxing to the Yuemiao Temple in Xiaoshan, while passing the Zunyi Bridge, suddenly

Page 18

encountered several bandits who ordered it to stop. They immediately boarded the boat and thoroughly searched it. All the male and female, old and young pilgrims, totaling over thirty people, were searched one by one, and none were spared. However, as the amount of silver was not much, they stripped all the pilgrims of their clothes, resulting in a total loss estimated at over two hundred yuan.

In the news above, we get a sense that so-called divine authority, so-called spiritual efficacy, are nothing more than deceptive tricks. If not, those men and women who travel far with boundless enthusiasm to offer incense should not have received such an unpleasant experience!

Director Zhang of the Village

— Si Quan

In the courtyard, two tall osmanthus trees had already bloomed with branches full of golden flowers in the early autumn season, but the weather was as hot as in the middle of summer. Passersby outside the wall often rested at the foot of the wall, and the rich fragrance inexplicably comforted their senses. Even more, some leaned against the wall and comfortably dozed off. The children nearby loved these tiny flowers even more, but Director Zhang's prestige in the town made them afraid to brazenly ask the adults to fetch them, so they often climbed in from the corner of the wall at great risk to pick them secretly.

Facing the courtyard was Director Zhang's bedroom. Every day, after smoking his fill of opium, he would hide behind the window curtains with his wife's maid, Qiuxiang, deliberately watching the children stealing on the high wall, taking it as amusement. Qiuxiang was even more clever at guessing the director's thoughts, so Director Zhang's days were naturally very comfortable.

His first wife was a virtuous woman who, after more than ten years of marriage, had not borne him a son or daughter. She felt that a woman who failed to fulfill her duty of bearing children was letting her husband down. She also suspected that she had committed some injustice in her previous life, resulting in her childlessness in this life. She told the director her thoughts and, on one hand, hired workers to build a Buddhist hall next to their house, and on the other hand, advised the director to take her dowry maid as a concubine, so that she could piously worship Buddha and cultivate blessings for her next life.

Director Zhang had long harbored improper thoughts about Qiuxiang, but he had been hindered by his wife's eyes and had only dared to touch her secretly on more than one occasion. Now, following his wife's orders, he had the study in the back courtyard renovated, planting seasonal flowers and plants throughout the courtyard, and locking himself in his bedroom every day. However, as the director of the town, his affairs and revenue were equally troublesome. In the past, he used to go to the teahouse every afternoon, which was almost his office, because by that time, all the tea drinkers had left, and those who waited there with unpleasant faces were all Director Zhang's clients. From the flow of money to heinous crimes, everything depended on Director Zhang's word to determine right and wrong. Moreover, his judgments were the law, and no one dared to utter a single objection. Besides, Director Zhang himself had said that he was an honest official and had never wronged anyone. This reputation of Director Zhang and his income simultaneously dominated the highest power in the town.

Since he had acquired Qiuxiang, he entrusted this important responsibility to his trusted follower, Zhang Er Ye. Zhang Er Ye's original name was Agou, and he was Director Zhang's tenant farmer. It was said that he had a beautiful wife who, after being raped by Director Zhang, committed suicide out of shame, and only then did Agou become Director Zhang's follower. However, Agou had a nimble mouth and a shrewd mind. He did not resent Director Zhang for forcing his wife to her death, but instead catered to his master's wishes in every way, committing all kinds of evil deeds. As a result, Zhang Er Ye's name spread. In fact, this was the intention of others who cursed him as Director Zhang's son. Agou did not think so thoroughly. Hearing the words "Zhang Er Ye," he beamed, naturally pleasing his master, Director Zhang, even more.

These days, the wife was sick, and Qiuxiang had gone to the Buddhist hall. Agou was always waiting in the director's room. To relieve the director's loneliness, he came up with an idea that made the director jump up from the opium bed like a spring.

The sun had already set, and Director Zhang, after smoking an excessive amount of opium, still felt unwell all over. The osmanthus flowers in the courtyard, like a charming woman, tempted him. "Damn it, why isn't she back yet!" He clenched his right fist, hitting his own left hand, and slowly paced to the front, unexpectedly bumping into a short figure at the side of the door.

"Director, Agou deserves to die!" Zhang Er Ye's figure seemed even shorter.

"Why are you being so sneaky!" the director said with a smile. "Did it succeed?" Then he turned back and walked towards the opium bed, and Agou followed closely like a shadow.

"Congratulations, Director! I spent half a day talking, using both soft and hard tactics... haha," he immediately lowered his voice and whispered into the director's ear, "Now, at my house..."

"You've worked hard, Agou!" The director pushed him onto the opium bed. "Have a puff!" While laughing, he stroked his upper lip and spun around the room.

When There's Food to Eat

— Qing Quan

Da Ben Zhen

— Li Ni

Here, there is only a long and wide road, lying quietly in the scorching sun of the southern country, as if in a state of extreme fatigue. A gust of wind swept by, and suddenly waves of rolling dust surged from the ground, hazy like the yellow sandstorms of winter in the northern country, making people's eyes very uncomfortable. The Ben Zhen River flows year-round with peach-red water, gently rippling, like a bed of brocade, winding leisurely, crossing this long road, interweaving into a cross shape. A tall wooden bridge spans the river, connecting the road, allowing cars and trucks to rumble across the bridge. The heavy trucks make a rumbling sound that often startles people from their sweet dreams in the tranquil afternoon, causing them to open their sleepy eyes and look at the scorching blue sky, suspecting that it is the city noise before a storm.

When the road directly from Da Ben Zhen to Singapore was not yet completed a few years ago, there were regular small steamers traveling between Singapore. The transportation of all goods depended entirely on this beautiful and secluded Ben Zhen River with its peach-red waters. Now that land transportation has been completed, the small steamers have lost their original position and power and have been eliminated. Only the small pier on the river still stands alone, as if refusing to accept its fate, glaring at the tall wooden bridge.

From the appearance of Da Ben Zhen, it hardly seems to be a commercial port. There are no towering chimneys spewing light and wispy smoke; there are no majestic buildings; even the flickering electric lights are absent; not to mention its entertainment venues. Here, there is only this unique long and dusty road. Along the river, a section is dotted with a hundred or so low and simple attap houses, which are where the overseas Chinese gather to buy and sell, forming this small "Shan Ba" "rural" town.

In addition to these hundred or so shops, Da Ben Zhen is surrounded by vast and towering betel nut and rubber trees, green like a vast blue sea, standing neatly. Rubber and betel nuts are their main products each year, and they are also the lifeline that constitutes the commercial prosperity of this small town. However, the drastic drop in rubber prices in recent years, the sluggishness, and the poor harvest of betel nuts have made the commerce of this small town even more desolate!

It can be said that the natives of Da Ben Zhen are completely assimilated by the overseas Chinese. No trace of their crude barbarity remains. Their customs are simple, they are extremely warm and sincere to people, and they have a spirit of courtesy, showing the demeanor of people from civilized countries.

Every time in the quiet night, when all sounds are silent, I always like to drag my wooden slippers alone, walking rhythmically on the wooden bridge over the Ben Zhen River, leaning on the railing, admiring the full and bright moon in the mid-sky, counting the twinkling stars, and reminiscing about my distant homeland, or looking at the faint shadows of the bushes on both sides of the river, and the light fishing boats as light as feathers, shuttling back and forth under the bridge, singing oars, and disappearing like smoke in a short while.

Sometimes, when the mournful and melancholic Malay music mixed with heart-wrenching soft songs is intermittently transmitted from the distant yachts, the tragic tone lingering in my ears vibrates my heartstrings, often evoking the desolate emotions in my heart, and I shed tears of sadness!

However, the beautiful, tranquil, and secluded atmosphere of Da Ben Zhen, like an ancient town, when recalled at this time, makes me yearn for it endlessly.

Broadcasting News

Nightingale’s Cai She Liulang is starting to compile “Nightingale Songs”, the content includes modern pop songs and out-of-print famous songs, a total of thirty songs, all equipped with more accurate sheet music. The prelude is a “Nightingale Song” composed by the society’s Fan Zhenjun. The cover is printed with exquisite photos. The price is fifteen cents per book. The period before the 20th of this month is the reservation period. For mail order, the shipping fee is one cent in this city, and one cent two cents for other cities, limited to one cent, two cents and five cents. You can order from Dunben Radio Station, No. 1 Zilan Village, Minquan Road, Dongxin Bridge, or Dahua Radio Station in the World, or Huaxing Radio Station, No. 19 Qingdao Road, Nightingale Art.

Broadway Music Singing Society is now jointly hired by Yili Soda Company and Taiping Moving Company to broadcast programs. It will be broadcast on the Navigation Radio Station from 3:00 to 4:00 every day starting from Xingxian. Those who like to listen to good songs, please pay attention (1180,000 rate). If you want to request a song, please call (90000) Taiping Moving Company.

Movie News

Star News Zero

(1) Hu Jia asked for leave to travel to Hong Kong and unfortunately contracted pneumonia. He has now been admitted to Dr. Wei's Hospital in Hong Kong for treatment. Once he recovers, he will return to Shanghai to cancel his leave.

(2) Shen Xiling's directed film "Nostalgia" had a surprising success at the test screening at the Central Grand Theatre. The film will be released soon.

(3) Zhang Shichuan's directed sound dialogue film "The Big Family" has been filming in the Star Second Studio for days, and the work is very intense.

(4) Zheng Zhengqiu, Li Pingqian, and Wu Cun have been working hard in the directing department for days, writing new works, and now most of them have been completed.

(5) Xu Xinfu's new work "Jade Horse" is a detective film against drugs. It stars Yan Yuexian, Gong Jianong, and Wang Zhengxin. The whole play is full of tension and can be compared with imported films.

(6) The new studio of Star Company is about to begin construction.

(7) Zhou Jianyun and his wife and Ms. Hu Die arrived in Geneva on the 6th of this month. "Sister Flowers" and "Orchid in an Empty Valley" and other films were shown publicly in the area. The Chinese representative office of the League of Nations held a banquet for Zhou Hu on the 7th, and the situation was extremely warm. Zhou Hu planned to stay in Geneva for two days and then travel to Rome. They will leave Europe and return to China on the Luso around the 13th.

Shen Xiling's Third Creation "Nostalgia"

In the far away Northeast, the beautiful family of Gao Zhipin was scattered and displaced by the fire. She took her elderly mother and a neurotic hunchbacked servant and drifted to Shanghai. Intoxicated with paper and drunk, she sat singing all night. Shanghai's prosperity remained the same. While suffering from the oppression of life, they watched the walking dead intoxicated with life and death. A piece of nostalgia aroused Gao Zhipin's infinite grief and indignation. Later, after experiencing vicissitudes, she finally solved the problem of life, but Shanghai was not a place to live and work in peace. She encountered a second upheaval.

"Nostalgia" seriously tells us that if each of us is living a life of intoxication and muddleheadedness, then everyone is in danger of losing their home at any time.

This is Shen Xiling's third creation. In Nostalgia, he entrusted his infinite sorrow for his homeland with the strong sense of justice of a poet.

The "Downtown" in "Goddess of Freedom" is completely "sealed off" due to the economic downturn

Business is indeed difficult to do this year. Everywhere they are clamoring for "big discounts" and "big auctions," but they are still experiencing an economic downturn everywhere. Unexpectedly, this economic downturn has been reflected like an infectious disease in the third sound film "Freedom God" of the Electric Communications Company. It turned out that when "Freedom God" was shooting the Guangzhou street rain scene last night, shops suddenly sprang up in the open-air studio. Fresh fruit shops, shoe stores, butcher shops, wine shops, etc., actually did business under the mercury lamps, and the newly opened shops were indeed twice as profitable, showing a sense of serving those who were unwilling. However, a torrential rain suddenly poured down, and the cameraman Yang Jimin's camera swept wildly, and all the essence of the "city" in "Freedom God" was in the "seal off".

After "The Beginning of Man"

"The Beginning of Man" is a masterpiece by Shi Dongshan of Yihua Film Company. It is currently being shown at the Jincheng Grand Theater and has garnered much praise from various newspaper film publications. The audience has been quite crowded in recent days. Following "The Beginning of Man," Jincheng has decided to screen Yue Ming's "Madness." "Madness" is starred by Wu Lizhu, our country's only martial arts star. In addition to all the dialogues and songs being voiced, it also features various colors such as red, yellow, and blue. It is both audible and visual. "Madness" has set a new record for domestic films, so film fans will definitely be scrambling to crowd the theater when it is released.

The Performing Arts Laboratory Enrolls Free Students

The "Performing Arts Laboratory" founded by playwright Liu Yawei and others is scheduled to officially begin classes on the 17th of this month, from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM. They are now continuing to recruit six free auditing students (female) and four (male). However, applicants must have a junior high school education or above and be at least sixteen years old to apply. It is said that an exam will be held at the laboratory at 10:00 AM on the 16th (Sunday), and those who pass will join the official classes starting on the 17th. The address is No. 195, South Chenghaiwei, Chongqing Road, Shanghai International Settlement. It is also said that the application method for auditing students is by mail. The letters should be sent to the laboratory or the Social Evening News office, to be collected by Liu Yawei. However, the deadline is before the 16th.
